kha phye/ mtshan zum par 'gyur ba yin pa las/ padma gcig nyin mtshan thams cad du kha zum par gyur pa dang / de'i rgyu mtshan rgyal po la bsnyad pas/ de sras khyad par can
'khrungs pa'i ltas yin pas lags par gnyer gyis shig ces bsgo'o/ /de nas nam zhig na padma de kha phye ba'i nang nas khye'u mtshan dang ldan pa gcig byung nas slob dpon
klu sgrub ga na yod zer/ tshul de rgyal pos thos nas bur bzung ste skyed cher bsrings so/ /cher skyes pa na/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyi spyan sngar byon rab tu byung bsnyen
par rdzogs/ phyi mtshan nyid kyi sde snod thams cad la legs par sbyangs pas mkhas pa chen por gyur/ de nas dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur/ rgyud bshad/
gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa ma lus pa nod cing thos bsam mthar

phyin par mdzad nas slob dpon dang lhan cig dpal gyi ri la bzhugs so/ /de skad du yang bzhi brgya pa'i 'grel pa las/ 'di ltar slob dpon 'phags pa lha ni singga la'i gling du
'khrungs pa/ singga la'i rgyal po'i sras zhig ste mthar rgyal tshab bor nas de nyid du rab tu byung zhing / de nas lho phyogs kyi rgyud ltar 'ongs te/ slob dpon klu sgrub
kyi nye gnas nyid du gyur ces gsungs pa yin no/ /dus de'i tshe rgya gar shar phyogs na bud med nyi shu tsam zhig sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la gus par gnas so/ /bud med
gcig la bram ze'i rigs kyi khye'u gcig btsas/ cher skyes nas sgra tshad la mkhas par bslabs/ der ma nang pa yin pas nang pa la gzud par 'dod kyang / pha phyi pa yin pas mu
stegs dbang phyug chen po'i grub mtha' la bcug ste phyi rol pa'i grub mtha' la mkhas par sbyangs shing / dbang phyug bsgrubs pas zhal mngon sum du mthong ste khyod ci 'dod
zer ba la/ phyogs las rnam par rgyal bar 'dod do zhes zhus pas/ mngal skyes thams cad kyis thub par med par gyur cig ces mchog gi dngos grub dang / kho rang la sgra tshad
kyi shes rab thod rgal ba zhig dang / sring mo paNDi ta zhes bya ba sgra tshad kyi rtsod pa mkhas pa zhig dang / ne tso paNDi ta zhes pa sgra tshad la mkhas pa zhig
dang / the le skor paNDi ta zhes pa sa la bskyur ba tsam gyis sgra tshad sbyor ba'i yi ge rang bris su yong ba zhig ste thun mong gi dngos grub bzhi byin no/ /de bzhis ma
thub na nga rang snying gi dkyil du zhugs la byin gyis rlob bo

zhes khas blangs so/ /de nas rgya gar shar phyogs kyi nang pa'i paNDi ta rnams la 'o skol rtsod pa byed dgos/ khyed rgyal na nga rang chu bo ganggA la 'chir 'gro yi/ nga rgyal
na khyed rnams nga'i grub mtha' la 'jug dgos shing khyed kyi gtsug lag khang dang chos rnams kyang bsreg dgos zer te/ rtsod pa byas pas kho rgyal nas rgya gar shar phyogs
kyi sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa phal cher bshigs/ de bzhin rgya gar lho phyogs su'ang byas nas ma la ngas 'di ltar byas so zhes bsgrags pa dang / ma'i bsam pa la kye ma
'di nang pa'i paNDi ta zhig gis pham par byas nas nang pa'i bstan pa la btsud na ci ma rung snyam du bsam ste/ bu sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rta'i lus tsam la rgya gar shar
dang lho na rna ba tsam yang med/ de gnyis na nang pa'i paNDi ta mkhas par chud pa yang med/ de dag pham par byas pas khyod mkhas par yang mi cha/ bstan pa rdzogs pa dang
paNDi ta mkhas pa yul dbus nA lendra na yod pas/ de dag las rgyal na mkhas par 'gyur ba yin no/ /zhes smras pas/ kho nga rgyal skyes te/ de thams cad ming med par bcom
la mu stegs pa'i bstan pa la gzhug snyam ste/ yul dbus su phyin te/ gnas de na gardho la chen po bdun/ lha khang chen po bcu bzhi/ paNDi ta mkhas pa stong lnga brgya yod
pa rnams la/ khos nga mu stegs rta dbyangs bya ba yin khyed dang rtsod pa byed/ khyed rgyal na nga rang chu bo ganggA la 'chir 'gro/ nga rgyal na khyed rnams nga'i grub
mtha' la 'jug dgos shing / khyed kyi gtsug lag khang dang glegs bam

rnams kyang bsreg dgos/ de'i dpang po rgyal po la 'chol ba yin pas dus thob cig byas pas/ der nang pa rnams gros byas te/ 'di mdo nas bstan pa nyams par byed par lung bstan
pa yang yin zhing / rgya gar shar dang lho'i nang pa thams cad pham par byas 'dug pas/ 'o cag gis mi thub dpal gyi ri nas slob dpon klu sgrub yab sras spyan 'dren pa rigs
zer/ de'i bar la re zhig long yod par gyis shig de nas zhag sum cu na rtsod par bya yi zhes dus btab/ der khos kyang gzhan zhig sbron par shes te/ re zhig khyed dang rtsod
pa byed kyi/ phyi rol na yod pa nang du ma 'gro/ nang na yod pa phyir ma ldang zer zhing kho sgo la nyal nas phyi nang gi 'grul bcad do/ /dge 'dun rnams gdugs tshod gsol
ba'i bar la mgo la dbyu gus brdeg cing grangs byed do/ /der dge 'dun rnams kyis slob dpon yab sras spyan 'dren pa la mi phyin kyang dus la mi sleb/ chos skyong mgon po
la gsol ba gdab bo zhes gros byas nas zhu 'bul gyi 'phrin yig 'di ltar te/ shin tu khur dka' khur gyis lus dub khyu mchog rnams ni khyod la gsol 'debs na/ /kye ma rma med
nyid du rol pa 'ba' zhig gis ni rab tu 'khrug byed dam/ /'di na nus ldan gzhan med 'khor lo bying ba can gyi shing rta myur du drongs/ /lta zhing 'dug gam yun ring gnas
kyang 'di ni khyod kyi khur yin phrag la longs/ /zhes pa bris te gtor ma'i steng du bzhag nas mgon po la gsol ba btab pas/ bya rog gcig byung ste

'phrin yig mchus bzung ste 'phur te song nas/ des slob dpon yab sras la 'phrin yig de phul bas/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis gzigs te slob dpon 'phags pa lha la mu stegs rta dbyangs
kyis bstan pa nyams dmas par byas pa yod pa 'dug de ldog pa la nga 'gro gsungs pa dang / 'phags pa lhas zhal nas slob dpon gshegs mi 'tshal/ bdag phyin la de gdul lo
zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas khyod kyis mi thub gsungs pa la/ thub zhus pas blta yi gsungs nas slob dpon gyis mu stegs kyi grub mtha' bzung / ArYa de bas nang pa'i
grub mtha' bzung nas brtsad pas 'phags pa lha lan gsum rgyal nas mu stegs ngan pa de khyer gsungs nas mchil lham slob dpon la brgyab pas 'gyod pa skyes pa na/ slob dpon gyi
zhal nas/ de dus mu stegs kyi 'du shes yod pas nyes pa med/ da khyod kyis kho thul ba 'dug pas song zhig gsungs/ de nas yul dbus su rdzu 'phrul gyis byon pas/ lam du lha
mo gcig gis spyan slong ba la spyan ya gcig byin no/ /nA lendrar chu len la nga 'ongs so gyis byas pas/ chu len gyis nga 'ongs so zer ba'i btsun chung gcig 'dug smras
pas/ dge 'dun rnams na re/ de su yi sprul pa yin mi shes pas brtag par bya'o zhes chu lug gi rmig gang blugs nas btang pas/ slob dpon gyi des khrus byas chu ma god par ldog
btang byung bas/ 'phags pa yin par shes te/ chu len gyi cha lugs su rdzus la byon cig ces zhus pas/ de ltar mdzad nas byon pa'i tshe/ sngar nas chu

len gyis kho la phyag dgos pa las/ slob dpon gyis kho'i mgo la rdog pa bzhag nas byon/ der dge 'dun gyi gral gyi smad kyi char bzhugs pas/ khos bgrangs pa na grangs lhag nas/
sngar med pa'i mgo ldum gang nas 'ongs zer/ slob dpon gyis mgo ldum ske nas 'ongs byas pas/ khos rtsod pa byed par shes nas/ byi'u gcig changs par bzung nas/ 'di shi ba'am
ma shi ba yin zer/ de khyod la rag las so zhes gsungs pas/ kho them pa'i steng du 'dug nas nga nang na 'dug gam phyi na 'dug zer ba la/ yang slob dpon gyis khyod kyi
spyod lam la rag las zhes gsungs pas/ spobs pa lan med du gyur to/ /de nas dge 'dun rnams kyis sring mo dang ne tso dang the le skor paNDi ta gda' 'o zhes zhus pas/ de'i
gnyen por dge bsnyen ngo tsha med pa dang / byi la dang mar nag sta gon byas so/ /der sang rtsod pa byed pa'i do nub dbus su rgyal po/ g.yas su slob dpon/ g.yon du rta dbyangs
kyi khri bshams te kho'i khri'i steng du krad rnying la sogs pa'i mi gtsang ba bzhag nangs par khri la thams cad 'khod 'khor rnams kyang bsdad grub pas na/ kho na
re/ mig gcig pa 'di ci smra zhes smra ba la/ slob dpon gyis/ drag po mig gsum ldan yang de nyid mthong ba med/ /brgya byin mig stong ldan yang de nyid mthong ba med/ /ArYa
de wa mig gcig po ni gang yin des/ /srid pa gsum po ma lus pa yi de nyid mthong / /zhes gsungs pas/ der khos ral ba btegs te mig

gcig bstan pa dang / slob dpon gyis de la ngo mtshar che rgyu med ces gsungs nas zhabs kyi mthil nas kyang mig gcig bstan pas/ de nas kho na re/ khyod kyis nga'i rtsod zla
mi 'ong gi sring mo dang / ne tso dang / the le skor rnams kyi lan thob cig zer ba la/ slob dpon gyis dge bsnyen dang byi la dang mar nag rnams btang bas/ sring mo de dge
bsnyen ngo tsha med de mthong ba na ngo tsha nas gang yang smra ma nus/ ne tsos kyang byi la mthong ba na skrag nas gang yang ma nus/ the le skor gyi sa la sgra tshad kyi
yi ge rang bris su yong ba de mar nag pho bas thams cad nyams pa dang kho spobs pa lan med par gyur to/ /de nas rgyal po dpang du bzhag nas brtsad pas/ dang por kun gyis
go yang / ji zhig na grub mtha' shin tu cha phra bar gyur te/ rjes su brjod pa'i dpang pos rjes gcod ma nus/ shan 'byed pa'i dpang pos bshad ma phyed/ des stobs kyis rgyal
pos kyang tshar bcad rjes bzung gang yang ma shes pa dang / kho na re/ blun dpyad la dri zer nas glang rdzi bkug nas dris pas/ slob dpon rgyal zer/ yang kho na re/ rdzu
'phrul 'gran pas khyed rang nam mkhar dkyil 'khor bris/ ngas bsub bo/ /yang na ngas bri yi/ khyed rang bsub zer ba la/ kho 'drir bcug slob dpon gyis bsub bo/ /yang kho
na re/ yang na nga nam mkha' la 'phur/ yang na khyed rang 'phur zer ba la/ slob dpon gyis khyed rang 'phur gsungs pas/ khos rgyang ring por 'phur ba na/ slob dpon gyis

yum chen mo'i sku shin tu che ba zhig tu sprul nas pus mo'i lha nga'i 'og tu phyag gi thal mo bkab pas khos 'phur ma nus so/ /de ltar rtsod pa dang nus pa dang / rdzu 'phrul
gang la'ang 'gran ma nus par shin tu ngo tsha ste/ dbang phyug snying la zhugs te byin gyis rlob par khas blangs pa yang mi gtsang ba'i rdzas kyis 'khor ma nus pa dang
/ der kho na re/ mang po'i dbus su lhas bslus so zhes smre sngags bton nas/ sngar nga rgyal ches pas shin tu skyengs te tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du 'gro'o snyam ste bros so/
/slob dpon gyis kho bdas pas nam mkha' mthon po nas/ da khyod 'di nas yar 'gro na rlung spu gri can gyis lus dum bur gtub pa yod gsungs pas yod pa ci shes zer/ khyod rang
ral pa gcig chod la 'phangs dang gsungs pas khos de ltar byas pa na ral pa dum bu dum bur song pas kho bred de 'gro ma nus/ de nas kho khrid ral pa bregs shig gsungs pas/
kho na re/ ral pa mi 'breg nga rang chu bo ganggAr 'chir 'gro zer yang / ral pa bregs nas bka' sde snod mang po bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang zhig tu bcug ste bzhag pas/
kho skyo ste mdo rgyud bstan bcos khyad par can rnams bltas pas/ rang gi lta ba de nor ba dang / rgyu 'bras phyin ci log spyad pa'i sdig pas dmyal bar 'gro ba shes nas/
shin tu bya ba ma yin pa byas pa la 'gyod de/ nyes pa lce 'dis byas pas lce gcod zer te skye tshang nas spu gri blangs pas/ de ltar byed du ma ster bar/ de'i nub rmi lam
na sngar byas las la 'gyod pa skyes pas kyang sdig pa mang po byang la/ da nang pa sangs rgyas pa la

zhugs nas rgyu 'bras ston pa'i bstan bcos brtsams na sdig pa ches cher 'dag go zhes pa'i lung bstan byung pas/ mdo dran pa nyer bzhag sogs bltas te rgyu 'bras ston pa'i bstan
bcos dge ba bcu dang / rtsa ltung bcu bzhi pa dang / bla ma lnga bcu pa rnams brtsams/ zhes bu ston gyi gsang 'dus rgyud kyi bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed las bshad
do/ /rang lugs ni rtsa ltung bcu bzhi pa dang / bla ma lnga bcu pa gnyis 'dis mdzad par mi bzhed la/ gang ltar de lta bu'i mu stegs rta dbyangs de phyis su slob dpon dpa'
bo zhes bya bar gyur cing / 'di la pha khol zhes pa dang / ma khol zhes pa dang / ma ti tsi trar yang grags/ des rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi skyes rabs sogs bstan bcos
mang du mdzad/ 'phags pa yab sras la dbang dang gdams pa sogs nos thugs nyams su bzhes pas tshe 'di la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub brnyes so/ /de lta bu'i slob
dpon 'phags pa lha de ni rgyud du ma nas lung bstan te/ 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud las/ gzhan yang rab byung dam pa ni/ /singga la yi gnas na gnas/ /'phags pa min la 'phags pa'i
ming / /pha rol rgol ba bzlog nas ni/ /mu stegs rnams kyi sngags sun phyung / /zhes pa dang / dus 'khor rgyud phyi ma las/ dge bcu'i lam gyi grub par gyur pa 'phags pa'i
lha/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /slob dpon des pha rol phyin pa'i bstan bcos dbu ma bzhi brgya pa/ dbu ma lag pa'i tshad/ 'khrul pa bzlog pa'i gtan tshig

grub pa/ ye shes snying po kun las btus la sogs pa mang du mdzad cing / sngags phyogs la ni gong du bstan pa rnams so/ /yang dpal 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi thugs sras bzhi'i
nang tshan grub chen klu'i byang chub ni sngar slob dpon klu sgrub li kha ra shing 'phel du gser 'gyur mdzad dus rgan rgon gnyis slob dpon la dad pa skyes/ rgan pos slob
dpon gyi nye gnas byas pas rgan po shi nas ma he skyong ba'i bu zhig tu skyes/ cher longs pa na ma he 'tsho bar phyin pas sngar gyi bag chags dran te slob dpon gyi drung
du phyin te/ grub pa nga skyo bas sgom zhig slobs dang zer/ slob dpon gyis ma he sgoms gsungs nas btang pas/ des kyang slob dpon gsungs pa bzhin ma he bsgoms pas/ shin tu
gsal ba byung / re zhig na slob dpon gyi drung du 'ongs nas/ da nga'i rwa 'di sgo la gtugs kyin mi bde zer ba na/ yang slob dpon gyis/ da sgom de dor la mdun du mi dkar
po zhig sgoms gsungs pas/ yang de bzhin bsgoms pas de gsal bar byung nas dngos grub ci 'dod zer/ grub pa la dri yi byas nas/ slob dpon gyi drung du phyin te 'di ltar byung
bas ci skad bya zer/ slob dpon gyis khyed rang nga'i snying la zhugs gyis shig gsungs/ de bzhin byas pas zhugs pa'i snang ba byung ste chos la chos kyi spyan rnam par dag
de nas rab tu byung bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan klu'i byang chub bam klu'i blor btags/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor du bcug dbang bskur/ rgyud bshad/ gdams pa dang
rjes su bstan pa ma lus

pa gnang zhing / 'dis gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil chog nyi shu pa sogs bstan bcos kyang 'ga' mdzad/ mthar dpal gyi ri la gshegs te deng sang yang bzhugs so/ /yang thugs sras bzhi'i
shAkya bshes gnyen nam shAkya mi tra ni gong du bstan pa ltar rim lnga'i rim pa gnyis pa mdzad mkhan de yin/ yo ga ba shAkya bshes gnyen bya ba de dang 'di mi gcig
ste/ yo ga ba des legs ldan 'byed kyi lung mang po drangs shing 'di ni klu sgrub kyi thugs kyi sras mchog tu gyur pa zhig yin la/ legs ldan 'byed ni klu sgrub kyi dngos slob
tsam yin kyang / sras kyi thu bo min pas de'i bstan bcos nas lung 'dren mdzad pa mi 'byung bas so/ /yang spyod bsdus la 'grel pa mdzad mkhan gyi shAkya bshes gnyen bya
ba gcig byung ba de yang 'di dang mi gcig cing / gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs pa'i brgyud 'dzin shAkya bshes gnyen zer ba zhig yod pa de dang yang dus mi 'grigs pas mi
gcig par bshad pa yin no/ /yang ma tang gi pa ni 'jigs pa'i dur khrod du brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mdzad pas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi zhal gzigs/ yul las mtshan du btags
pa la rnal 'byor dbang phyug paN ta pa/ rigs kyi sgo nas mtshan thogs pa la ting go pa phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub brnyes kyang sbas pa'i brtul zhugs la gnas
pa gsang mtshan mtshan gsang ba zhes grags pa zhig yin par bshad pa yin no/ /yang nye sras sangs rgyas bskyang legs ldan 'byed gnyis ni slob dpon 'di'i dbu ma'i

bshad srol gtso bor 'dzin pa ste/ de yang rtsa ba shes rab las/ bdag las ma yin gzhan las min/ /zhes sogs dam bca' bzhi gsungs pa la/ sgrub byed kyi rigs pa thal 'gyur gyi
rigs pa'i sgo nas bsgrub rigs par sangs rgyas bskyang gis gsungs nas/ lugs de la dbu ma thal 'gyur bar grags/ legs ldan 'byed kyi sangs rgyas bskyang gi bzhed pa de bkag
nas rang rgyud kyi rigs pa'i sgo nas bsgrubs pas dbu ma rang rgyud par grags te/ mdor na dbu ma thal rang zhes pa'i kha skad 'di slob dpon de gnyis nas byung ba yin no/ /yang
nye sras dpa' bo ni/ gong du bstan pa ltar rta dbyangs yin no/ /yang dngos slob tu 'dod pa ltar na sras kyi gtso bo bzhi'i nang tshan nam/ dgongs pa skong ba'i slob
ma zla ba grags pa ni dag pa'i snang bar 'phags pa klu sgrub la chos gsan cing rtsod dus kyi paNDi ta khyad par can zhig ste/ de yang spyir de dus nA lendra na paNDi ta mang
du yod kyang / mu stegs byed kyi rgol ba tshar gcod mi nus na phyir chos mi 'chad pa la/ slob dpon zla ba grags pas ni phyir chos 'chad nus pa las/ de'i tshe rgya gar
lho phyogs kyi mkhas pa chen po tsandra go mi slob dpon 'di yi drung du 'ongs te 'dud pa ma byas par bsdad pa dang / zla grags kyi thugs dgongs la rtsod dam bgro bar 'dod
pa gcig 'dir 'ongs pa yin te 'ong snyam nas/ phyogs gang nas 'ong / chos ci shes dris pas/ lho phyogs nas 'ongs/ sgra pA ni/ sher phyin tshul brgya lnga bcu pa/ 'jam dpal
mtshan brjod shes zer bas/ sgra dang mtshan nyid kyi rtsa ba dang / sngags

kyi rtsa ba smos pas lung rigs la mkhas par khas blangs kyang tshig khengs bskyungs par 'dug pas/ 'di tsandra go mi yin nam snyam ste ming dris pas/ tsandra zhes 'jig rten
pa rnams 'dogs so zer/ 'o na paNDi ta chen po thog babs su byon pa mi legs/ bsu ba bya dgos pas re zhig phyir byon cig phyir bsu ba bgyid do zhes gsungs nas chos 'chad 'phro
bcad/ gaNDI brdungs nas paNDi ta rnams bsags/ 'dir mkhas pa chen po tsandra go mi byon gyi bsu ba bya dgos kyi shing rta gnyis shoms la gcig la 'jam dpal gyi sku bzhugs/
gcig la tsandra go mi bzhugs la mchod pa'i tshogs kyis spyan drongs shig ces bsgos te/ 'jam dpal gyi sku la slob dpon tsandras 'jam dbyangs la phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs
pa bye ba rnams kyis bstod par gyur mod/ /de lta na'ang bsam pa blun po bla ma la gus zhes sogs kyis bstod pas/ de dges te slob dpon la 'jam dbyangs kyi zhal phyir
gzigs pas/ da lta yang na lendra na byin rlabs che zhing 'jam dbyangs mjing yon du grags pa bzhugs zhes grag go /der nA lendrar byon bsnyen bkur/ zla grags dang gdan 'dzom/
phan tshun chos kyi bgro ba mdzad pas/ zla grags kyis gang dris pa'i lan thogs med du btab/ tsandras spyan ras gzigs la dri zhing lan thogs bcas su thebs/ zla grags kyis
bltas pas spyan ras gzigs rdo sku bzhugs pa'i khang pa nas byung nas/ lan cig der song nas rgyab nas mnyan pas rdo sku nyid sprul skur mdzad nas chos 'chad kyin 'dug pa
dang / zhal blta dgos snyam nang du phyin pas sprul sku zhal brtul te/ der slob dpon

kyis sa the btsugs te/ 'phags pa la nye ring mnga' 'am/ khong la zhal ston pa ltar bdag la yang bstan du gsol zhes gsol ba btab pas/ mtshan mo rmi lam du byon te/ khyod 'jam
dpal gyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i mkhas pa chen po yin pas/ ngas byin gyis rlob mi dgos/ tsandra go mi la cung zad byin gyis brlabs pa yin gyi/ de skad ma zer bar song gsungs/
gnyid sad tshe/ de ltar lags kyang zhal ston pa zhu zhus pas/ spyan ras gzigs kyis zhal mngon sum du bstan pa dang / zla bas da bdag gi spyi gtsug tu bzhugs la sems
can thams cad kyis mthong bar mdzod cig ces gsol bas/ ngas sems can thams cad kyi drung du song yang / de rnams las kyi sgrib pas mthong bar mi 'gyur gsungs/ cis kyang bzhugs
shig ces gsol te 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug spyi bor khyer nas grong khyer chen po rnams su/ bdag gi spyi bo na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs bzhugs so/ /thams cad
kyis phyag dang mchod pa gyis shig ces bsgrags pa dang / la las ni gcig kyang ma mthong / la las khyi ro gcig mthong / phal che bas chos mang po bshad pas rlung smyo yin
zer/ chang 'tshong ma zhig gis zhabs tsam mthong bas kyang thun mong gi dngos grub thob ces grag go /de lta bu'i slob dpon des kun rdzob kyi snang ba thams cad brdzun par
mnyam gsungs pas/ paNDi ta rnams na re/ 'o na dngos po'i ba la 'o ma 'byung ba ltar/ ri mo'i ba la yang 'o ma 'byung ngam zer ba la/ 'byung gsungs te ri mo'i ba las 'o ma
bzhos pas byung / gtsug lag khang gi rdo'i ka ba 'di stong pa yin nam zer ba la yin

gsungs nas rdo'i ka la phyag brgyab pas thogs pa med par thal byung du mdzad pa sogs yod tan dpag tu med pa mnga' ste/ tshig gsal dang / 'jug pa'i gsham du slob dpon zla ba
grags pa mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje mnga' ba/ ri mor bris pa'i ba drus ma las 'o ma bzhos pas bden par zhen pa zlog par mdzad pa zhes sogs gsungs pas so/
/'o na slob dpon zla ba grags pa 'di klu sgrub kyi dngos slob yin nam snyam na/ 'di la mkhas pa so so'i bzhed pa dgod pa dang / rang lugs 'thad phyogs ngos bzung ba dang
gnyis las/ dang po ni/ jo bo rje'i gsung las/ klu sgrub slob ma zla grags yin/ /de las brgyud pa'i man ngag yod/ /ces gsungs pa shes byed du byas nas bka' gdams pa rnams
dngos slob yin par 'chad/ de bzhin du bu ston rin po ches gsang 'dus rgyud kyi bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed las/ slob dpon de klu sgrub kyi dngos slob min zer ba ni mi
'thad de jo bos mdzad pa'i bden gnyis las/ klu sgrub slob ma zla grags yin/ /de las brgyud pa'i man ngag yod/ /ces pa dang / slob dpon klu sgrub kyis kyang / slob ma'i
tha ma zla grags la/ /chos kyi tha ma skye med bstan/ /zhes gsungs pas so zhes gsungs nas/ zla grags dngos slob yin par bzhed/ chos rje ri bo dge ldan pa'i dngos slob yin
te/ zla grags tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa'i phyir zhes zer/ mkhas pa'i dbang po mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos gtan tshigs chos 'byung lhag bsam rab dkar las/ kho bo ni
zla grags klu sgrub kyi zhabs zin yin par sems te/ gsang

'dus sgron gsal las/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rim gnyis gnas kyi rgyas btab de ni klu sgrub las rnyed pa/ /khyab bdag dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpar btud de zla ba grags pas rim bzhin
bshad/ /ces dang / paNDi ta skal ldan grags pas/ de ni dpal ldan klu sgrub las rnyed pa zhes smos te/ de ni dpal ldan klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas kyi dngos kyi slob ma
nyid du so sor ston gyi brgyud pas ni ma yin no zhes sogs bshad cing / do ha mdzod kyi Tikka 'ga' zhig las kyang / zla grags kyis klu sgrub las man ngag dngos thob cing
/ mthar klu sgrub kyis dbu sbyin par btang nas bde ba can du gshegs pa'i tshe/ nA ga bo dhi/ ArYa de wa/ zla grags gsum gyis gsol ba btab pas/ sku ci 'dra ba'i 'od cig snang
bar byas nas/ gar yang ma rtog cir yang ma sems par/ /bcas bcos med pa'i rang bzhin nal mar zhog /ma bcos skye med rang rig byang chub sems/ /de ltar rtogs na sangs
rgyas de rang yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i gdams pa gnang zhes sogs dang / de'i tshe ArYa de was/ 'gro'o ArYa de wa 'gro/ /'od lus dag pa'i zhing du 'gro/ /song cig nA ga bo dhi
song / /ri bya rkang can du 'phur te song / /song cig zla ba grags pa song / /dpal gyi ri la thogs med song / /zhes sogs gsungs shing / zla ba grags pas kyang / chad do
zla ba grags pa chad/ /klu sgrub gshegs pas lam mkhan rgyun thag chad/ /ma bcos skye med chos kyi rgyun thag chad/ /yid la mi byed chos kyi rgyun thag chad/ /ces smras nas
dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi ri la bzhud ces sogs bshad

pas so/ /zhes sogs gsungs na zla grags klu sgrub kyi dngos slob yin pa lta bu zhig bzhed/ yang rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gsung rgyun gung rus 'bri bar mdzad pa'i
gsang 'dus rnam bshad las/ 'o na zla ba grags pa 'di klu sgrub kyi dngos slob yin nam zhe na/ 'phags pas rgyal bu la dbu sbyin par btang rjes zhal mjal ba lta bu la ni
'gal ba med de/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan pa'i rjes su zhal mjal ba dang / grub chen klu byang lho phyogs dpal gyi ri la da dung yang tshe'i rig 'dzin
brnyes nas bzhugs pa skal ldan rnams deng sang yang zhal mjal ba yin no/ /'phags pas dbu sbyin par ma btang gong du dpon slob tu byas nas 'chad nyan byas pa'i dpon slob
ni min te/ zla grags 'di nA ro pa'i bla ma tsandra go mi dang dus mtshungs su bshad pa dang / zla grags kyi dus na ArYa de ba'i slob ma gnas brtan chos skyong ste birWa
pa yang byon zin par bshad pa dang / klu sgrub dang de'i dngos slob phal cher yang 'das zin par zla grags rang nyid gsungs te zhes gsungs nas/ 'jug pa rang 'grel nas lung
'dren yang mdzad cing / srad bu kun blo'i gsang 'dus rgyud bshad sngon 'gro zin bris las/ dngos slob tu 'dod pa la lung rigs kyi gnod byed mang du brjod nas rang gi bzhed
pa la/ des na zla grags kyis klu sgrub kyi zhabs dus kyi dbang du byas na ma zin pa yin la/ phyis zhal bstan nas byin gyis brlabs pa ni ma bkag go zhes gsungs pas/ rje
btsun kun dga' bzang po yab sras rnams ni dngos slob min par bzhed do/ /gnyis pa rang lugs 'thad pa'i phyogs ngos bzung ba ni/ de ltar

mkhas pa'i bzhed pa mi mthun pa mang du yod pa de dag las/ bka' gdams pa rnams jo bo de ltar gsungs pas dngos slob yin gsungs pa mi rigs te/ zla ba grags pa de slob dpon klu
sgrub kyi dgongs pa phyin ci log pa skong ba'i brgyud pa'i slob ma yin pa la dgongs nas/ klu sgrub slob ma zla grags yin zhes gsungs pa yin gyi/ dngos slob tu ston pa ma
yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bu ston gyis sngar gyi jo bo'i lung de dang klu sgrub kyi lung drangs nas dngos slob tu bzhed pa la yang legs par brtags na 'thad phyogs ma yin te/
jo bo'i lung gi don ni gong du bstan zin la/ klu sgrub kyis lung de skye med mdzod nas yin pas/ skye med mdzod ni klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa ma yin par bu ston rang gi chos
'byung las bshad nas/ rgyud bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed las/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis kyang zhes gsungs nas skye med mdzod kyi lung drangs pas/ skye med mdzod klu sgrub
kyis mdzad pa yin par bzhed 'dug pas nang 'gal bas so/ /des na nang 'gal gyi gsung gis gzhan lugs 'gog cing rang lugs bsgrub pa ni mkhas pa'i zhal nas 'byung rigs pa'i
gtam ma yin no/ /ri bo dge ldan pa'i gsung de la ni rnam dpyad gtan nas ma byung ste/ zla grags tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa yin kyang / zla grags ma byon gong du klu sgrub
'das zin pas/ zla grags kyis tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa des/ klu sgrub sngon du 'das zin pa'i dngos slob yin pa la gcig kyang phan rgyu mi 'dug pa'i phyir ro/ /yang mkhas
pa'i dbang po klu sgrub rgya mtshos lung rigs kyi sgrub byed gong du

bkod pa de dag dang / yang chos 'byung lhag bsam rab dkar kyi bstan pa phyi dar gyi skabs na/ 'on kyang rig pa'i khu byug zla grags kyi zhabs zin yin la/ a ti sha rig pa'i
khu byug gi dngos slob yin zhing / nag tshos jo bo spyan 'dren la phyin pa'i tshe yang / rig pa'i khu byug bzhugs par rnam thar dang lam yig dag na gsal bas/ de dag gi lo
grangs brtsis na mi 'grigs pa ltar snang ste/ zhes sogs gsungs nas/ des na kho bos lung rig gi legs bshad sngar bshad pa ltar/ klu sgrub kyis lo drug brgya las ches lhag
pa zhig bzhugs pa'am/ yang na dag pa'i snang ba kho nas zhal mjal ba gang rung las ma 'das par khas blang par bya ste/ chos kyi rjes su 'brang pa'i rnam dpyod kyi dpyad
pa las de kho na ltar mthong ba'i phyir ro zhes gsungs pa de dag la brtags na/ sgron gsal sogs kyi lung drangs nas/ zla grags kyi dngos slob yin par bsgrub pa mdzad pa ni
mkhas pas dpyad dgos pa'i legs bshad du snang na yang / de'i rjes su zla grags klu sgrub kyi zhabs zin yin na/ rig pa'i khu byug zla grags kyi zhabs zin yin pa dang / jo
bo rje rig pa'i khu byug gi dngos slob yin pa rnams dus mi 'grig tshul gsungs pa rnams la dpyad pa 'di ltar 'jug ste/ zla grags klu sgrub kyi zhabs zin yin pa'i kha tshon
ni mkhas pa'i dbang po nyid kyis bcad zin/ zla grags kyi zhabs rig pa'i khu byug gis zin par ni chos 'byung du ma nas bshad cing yongs su grags pas 'di la snyon du med
la/ jo bo chen po rig pa'i khu byug gi slob ma yin par rnam thar dang / nag tshos

jo bo rje spyan 'dren par phyin pa'i lam yig na gsal bar bshad pas de yang dgag par mi nus shing / des na ston pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo bzhi brgya na klu sgrub byon nas
lo drug brgya bzhugs pa yin pa la ni rtsod pa cher med/ zla grags kyis lo lnga brgya bzhugs pa tsam zhig bshad kyis/ de las lhag pa bzhugs pa'i bshad tshod mi snang / rig
pa'i khu byug gis lo sum brgya bzhugs/ de'i slob ma a ti sha yin pas/ klu sgrub ston pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo stong 'das pa'i tshe mi bzhugs pa ni gong gi lo grangs brtsis
pas shes/ de nas zla grags kyis dgung lo lnga brgya/ de'i steng du rig pa'i khu byug gis dgung lo sum brgya bsnan pas brgyad brgya ste ston pa 'das nas lo stong dang
brgyad brgya nas jo bo rje byon par khas len dgos byung la/ de ni mi rung ste/ jo bo rje ni ston pa 'das nas lo sum stong lhag tsam 'das pa na byon pa yin par bstan rtsis
dang lo rgyus tshad ldan thams cad las bshad pas so/ /de bas na klu sgrub kyi dngos slob zla grags/ des lo lnga brgya bzhugs/ de'i slob ma rig pa'i khu byug des lo sum
brgya bzhugs/ de'i slob ma jo bo rje/ de nyid ston pa mya ngan las 'das nas stong phrag gsum lhag pa tsam na byon gsungs pa 'di dus mi 'grig pas 'thad pa'i gnas su ma mchis/
ci ste klu sgrub kyis lo drug brgya lhag bzhugs pas skyon med snyam na/ des kyang skyon spong mi thub ste/ klu sgrub kyis lo drug brgya las lhag pa stong tsam bzhugs
pa yin na'ang / zla grags kyis klu sgrub kyi zhabs zin rgyu ma byung bas/ rig pa'i khu byug gi dngos slob ma yin pa'am/ rig pa'i khu byug la che chung gnyis su mdzad na
'grig tsam yong ngam gsungs

pa sogs kyi thugs kyi ngal ba de lta bu mi mdzad par zla grags klu sgrub kyi dgongs pa skong ba'i slob ma yin gyi/ dus mtshungs kyi dngos slob ma yin zhes bdag nyid chen po
sa paN gyis gsungs pa 'di dang rjes su mthun pa zhig mdzad par zhu zhes mkhas dbang khyed la thal mo sbyor ro/ /des na zla grags klu sgrub kyi dngos slob yin na/ zla grags
nyid kyis/ bde ba can du klu sgrub gshegs par gyur pa des mdzad pa'i/ /gzhung mang dang ni slob ma'i tshogs de dag kyang dus nam zhig na nyams par 'gyur/ /de nyid nyi
ma nub pas deng sang gzhung lugs gsal po de ni gang na'ang med/ /ces zla grags kyi dus na klu sgrub kyi slob ma'i tshogs rnams kyang nyams pa ste 'das zin cing / de nyid
slob ma dang bcas pa gshegs pas zla grags kyi dus na gzhung lugs gsal po yang med gsungs pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu brgyud las 'ongs dang bdag gis rnam phye las rnyed gang
/ /zhes klu sgrub las dngos su ma gsan par gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de gsan par bshad pa sogs mi 'thad par 'gyur ro/ /rgyu mtshan de dag gi phyir na zla grags klu sgrub
kyi zhabs ma zin par rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rgyun las 'byung ba'i tshul gong du bkod pa de dag dang / khyad par bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta chen po la/ 'chad
ka nam mkha' 'bum gyis zla ba grags pa klu sgrub la sleb bam zhes zhus pa'i lan du/ klu sgrub kyi dgongs pa skong ba'i slob ma yin pas/ klu sgrub slob ma zla grags yin/ /zhes
gsungs pa lags zhes gsungs pa ltar/ zla grags klu sgrub kyi dgongs pa phyin ci ma log par skong ba'i slob ma yin

gyi/ zhabs zin ma yin pa'i phyogs 'di 'thad ldan yin pas/ ston pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo bzhi brgya na klu sgrub byon/ des lo drug brgya bzhugs/ dgu brgya na thogs med byon
nas dgung lo lnga brgya bzhugs pa'i sku tshe'i smad kyi slob ma dbyig gnyen yin par bshad cing / zla ba grags pa'i tshe/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen dang / phyogs glang dang
/ gnas brtan chos skyong ste birWa pa rnams kyang 'das zin par zla ba grags pa nyid kyis bshad pa'i phyir te/ 'jug pa rang 'grel las/ gal te gnas brtan dbyig gnyen dang
/ phyogs kyi glang po dang / chos skyong la sogs pa'i bstan bcos rnams kyi mdzad pa po byon zin par gyur pa de dag gis kyang yi ge tsam mthong bas 'jigs te/ rten cing 'brel
bar 'byung ba'i don phyin ci ma log par ston pa 'di yongs su spangs sam zhe na de skad du smra'o zhes gsungs pas so/ /'o na gsang 'dus sgron gsal las/ sangs rgyas kun
gyi rim gnyis gnas kyi rgyas btab de ni klu sgrub las rnyed pa/ /zhes pa dang / de'i 'grel pa paNDi ta skal ldan grags pas mdzad pa dang / do ha mdzod kyi TIka rnams las
dngos slob du bshad pa rnams ji ltar yin snyam na/ sgron gsal las de ltar bshad pa ni klu sgrub kyi man ngag la brten nas rnyed ces pa'i don yin te/ de yang klu sgrub kyi
zhabs zin nas 'chad nyan mdzad de man ngag dngos su thob pa ni ma yin gyis/ klu sgrub nas ArYa de wa sogs brgyud pa las brgyud pa las rnyed ces pa ste/ gcig nas gcig tu
brgyud pa las 'ong dang bdag gi rnam phye las rnyed gang / /zhes gsungs pas so/ /sgron gsal gyi

'grel pa skal ldan grags pas mdzad pa de las dngos slob tu bshad mod kyang / 'grel pa de ni tshad mar bu ston sogs kyi mkhas pa mang pos mi bzhed pa ltar don la yang gnas pas
'gal ba med do/ /gal te de rgya 'grel yongs grags yin pas tshad mar rigs so snyam na/ de la yang nges pa med de/ rgya gar gyi paNDi ta yin kyang 'khrul pa mnga' ba mang
du yod de/ slob dpon dbang phyug sde phyogs glang gi dngos kyi slob ma yongs grags kyi mkhas pa chen po yin kyang / phyogs glang gis mdzad pa'i tshad ma mdo'i don nor bar
bshad pa/ dpal ldan chos grags kyis lung 'gal gyi sgo nas bkag cing / klu sgrub kyi rim lnga'i rim pa gnyis pa'i mjug tu shAkya bshes gnyen gyi mdzad byang byung ba la
'khrul nas rgya gar ba 'ga' zhig gi shAkya bshes gnyen klu sgrub kyi mtshan gyi rnam grangs su bshad pa sogs rgya 'grel rnams la yang nor ba mang du yod pa'i phyir ro/ /do
ha mdzod kyi Tikka rnams las kyang dngos slob yin par bshad kyang / de yang lo rgyus tshad ma yin pa'i nges pa med cing / yin na yang des mi gnod cing / do ha mdzod kyi
Tikkar ma zad dbu ma'i brgyud rim 'ga' zhig las kyang / klu sgrub nas zla grags la brgyud tshul la nye gnas dngos grub brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor ba las brgyud tshul/ gzhung
bshad rgyud kyi mkhas pa paNDi ta las brgyud tshul/ rtsa ba klu sgrub nyid la dngos su thug tshul dang gsum du byas nas/ phyi ma la zla grags kyis klu sgrub la dngos su
thug tshul yang bshad mod cing / gzhan yang brgyud yig 'ga' zhig las/

klu sgrub/ zla grags/ des slob pa'i rdo rje la gdams zhes pa yang bshad mod/ de dag ni phyis su 'phags pas zhal bstan nas dag snang gi ngang la chos gsan pas/ de'i dbang du
mdzad nas brgyud pa'i rim pa la slob dpon gzhan ma smos par zla grags nyid kyis 'phags pa klu sgrub la dngos su gsan tshul smos pa yin pas/ 'di la 'gal ba cung zad kyang
yod pa ma yin de/ rje btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pas sa skya pa chen po la zhal dngos su bstan nas rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi bshad bka'/ lcags ri'i khong
las mi 'da' ba'i zab chos bzhi sogs stsal ba la brten nas/ gsung ngag nye brgyud la birWa pa nas gzhan mi dgos par sa chen nyid 'dren pa ni/ rang gzhan gyi grub mtha'i
zhal 'dzin thams cad rtsod med du bzhed pa'i phyir/ de las gzhan sa chen dang birWa pa dus mtshungs yong ba'i go skabs med do/ /gal te de dag mi mtshungs te/ sa chen la
birWa pas zhal bstan pa'i lo rgyus gsal bar yod/ zla grags la klu sgrub kyis zhal bstan pa'i lo rgyus kha gsal med pas so snyam na/ de'i lo rgyus rgyas pa yi ge'i rigs su
bris pa cher med kyang / don la klu sgrub kyis zla grags la zhal bstan pa la the tshom mi dgos ste/ klu sgrub lta bu'i bla mas zla grags lta bu'i brgyud 'dzin kyi slob
ma la zhal ston pa chos nyid yin te/ brgyud lugs gzhan la yang de lta bu'i tshul mang du snang ba'i phyir ro/ /gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi tas/ zla grags klu
sgrub kyi dgongs pa skong ba'i slob ma yin par gsungs nas/ yang rdog

lugs kyi dbang gi brgyud pa 'dren pa'i tshe/ klu sgrub kyis/ ArYa de ba/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa dang bzhi la stsal bar bshad pas 'thad ldan du
zhal gyis bzhes pas kyang don de nyid grub ste/ klu sgrub kyis zla ba grags pa la stsal tshul de dag pa'i snang ba tsam gyi sgo nas ma yin par dngos slob tu byas nas gdams
pa stsal ba yin na/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN rang nyid kyis dgongs pa skong ba'i slob mar ga la gsungs/ brgyud rim de yang 'thad ldan du mi bzhed dgos pa'i phyir ro/
/des na phyis zhal bstan nas dag pa'i snang bas mjal ba la ni nges pa med la/ de las gzhan dus kyi dbang du byas na zla grags kyis klu sgrub kyi zhabs zin yin pa la lung
rigs 'thad ldan med pas/ de'i dbang gis zla grags klu sgrub kyi dngos slob min pa 'di don la gnas so/ /zhes kho bo smra'o/ /gal te dag pa'i snang bar mjal nas gdams pa stsal
ba tsam gyi dngos slob tu 'gyur na/ mkhan chen g.yag pa'i mtshan can sangs rgyas dpal bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyi dngos slob tu khas len dgos te/ de la des zhal bstan
nas 'jam dbyangs dang sa paN sbags sgrub kyi gdams pa zab mo 'di stsal ba'i phyir te/ de ltar stsal ba'i gdams pa de mkhan chen des dngos slob rong ston shes bya kun rig
la gnang / rong ston nas brgyud pa'i gdams pa de kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges kyang gsan zhing / dus shig kun mkhyen chen po rong chung du chu'i steng du lhung ba'i tshe
chur ma nub pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i lo rgyus kun mkhyen chen po'i rnam thar na gsal zhing /

de yang gdams pa zab mo nyams su bzhes pa las byung bas chos de tshad ldan yin par deng sang rlung ltar grags pa'i phyir ro/ /mkhan chen g.yag pa chos rje sa paN gyi dngos
slob tu 'dod pa ni ha cang thal lo/ /de lta bu'i slob dpon zla ba grags pas/ sngags phyogs la gong du bstan pa de dag dang mtshan nyid phyogs la mngon pa mdzod dang / grub
mtha' rkang gcig pa'i phung po lnga'i rab byed dang / dbu ma la rtsa ba shes rab kyi don gyi 'grel pa 'jug pa/ tshig gi 'grel pa tshig gsal/ gzhan yang bzhi brgya pa'i
'grel pa dang / rig pa drug cu pa'i 'grel pa rnams mdzad do/ /de ltar 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi slob ma shAkya bshes gnyen/ 'phags pa lha/ klu'i byang chub/ sgra gcan 'dzin
dpal bshes gnyen te bzhi'i nang nas dang po gsum dang / zla grags dang bzhi char gyis slob pa'i rdo rje la gdams shing / 'di'i rnam thar gsal ba zhig ma mthong la/ des rjes
su bzung zhing byin gyis brlabs pa ni slob dpon nag pa po ste/ 'di la bu ston gyi gsang ba'i sgo 'byed las/ des nag po spyod pa la gdams/ de'i rnam par thar pa rgyas
pa bde mchog tu shes par bya zhing zhes sogs gsungs nas bde mchog pa'i nag po spyod pa'i rdo rje la bzhed/ 'gos lo chen pos nag po pa la che 'bring chung gsum du mdzad nas
'di chen po la bshad/ rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gsung rgyun zin bris 'ga' zhig las/ 'di la bus bde mchog pa'i nag po yin zer ba mi 'thad de dus mi mtshungs
pa'i

phyir ro/ /des na 'gos kyis nag po pa che 'bring chung gsum du byas nas 'di chen po zhes bshad kyang / 'di nag po spyod chung bya ba yin no zhes gsungs pas cung zad mi mthun
pa zhig go /'on kyang dus mi mtshungs pa'i phyir ro zhes pa ngor pa'i zin bris las bshad snang ba/ 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i brgyud rim la nag po pa nas/ nA ro pa'i
bar la/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa dang gsum/ lU hi pa'i brgyud pa la rnam rgyal gyi dod du bar ma'i slob dpon bsnan pas bla ma gsum byung bas/ gsang ba 'dus
pa'i brgyud rim la nag po spyod pa nas nA ro pa dang dus mtshungs mngon shes can gyi bar du sa 'dres pa las ma byung bas dus mi mtshungs gsung rgyu yin nam snyam pa 'thad
pa ltar snang yang / 'on kyang bde mchog mar lugs kyi brgyud pa la nag po pa nas/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ zhes bar der bla ma gcig gis chog pa zhig bshad/ de bzhin du gsang
'dus mar lugs grub thob gnyis kyi brgyud pa la yang / nag po spyod pa nas tai lo pa/ nA ro pa zhes dang / mkhas pa paNDi ta'i brgyud pa la/ nag po spyod pa nas/ dri med
blo gros/ des dpal ye shes snying po la gdams/ dpal ye shes snying po dang nA ro pa dus mtshungs pas/ nA ro pa dang nag po spyod pa ba'i bar du bla ma gcig gis chog pa
zhig mar lugs kyi brgyud yig rnams las byung zhing / zla grags dang / nA ro pa'i slob ma tsandra go mi dus mtshungs pas/ nA ro pa zla grags kyi zhabs zin na yang / zla grags
kyi

slob ma slob pa'i rdo rje/ de'i slob ma gsang 'dus brgyud pa nag po spyod pa ba'i zhabs zin pa tsam zhig khas len dgos pa 'dra mo zhig 'dug pas/ gsang 'dus pa'i nag po spyod
pa dang / bde mchog pa'i nag po spyod pa dus mi mtshungs pa'i kha tshon gcod pa yang dka' bar snang ngo / /gang ltar de lta bu'i nag po pa bde mchog brgyud pa'i nag po
pa yin na mgon po mngon byung gi rgyud dang / dus 'khor rgyud phyi ma rnams las lung bstan zhing rnam thar rgyas pa bde mchog chos 'byung rnams las 'byung ngo / /des dri
med blo gros dang / rgyal sras sa 'dres pa gnyis la gdams/ dang po des dpal ye shes snying po la/ de'i mar pa la brgyud pa'i tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ /gnyis pa rgyal sras sa
'dres pa chen po la slob ma'i mchog bIrYa bha dra ste mngon shes can/ de ba A ka ra tsandra ste za hor gyi mkhas pa btsun mo can/ dI paM ka ra ste mar me mdzad/ ratna a
ka ra shAnti ste dpal sbas dang bzhi la gsungs/ dang pos rim lnga la 'grel pa mdzad/ gnyis pas rim lnga'i gtor chog la sogs pa mdzad cing / mar me mdzad 'di ye shes zhabs
lugs pa'i brgyud 'dzin de'ang min la/ jo bo rje dang yang mi gcig go /de ltar lnga las mngon shes can gyis nag po dam tshig rdo rje la gdams/ de'i mtshan dngos shrI bha
dra zhes bya/ yang kha cig tu nag po dam tshig rdo rje rgya skad du smos pas kr-iShNa sa ma ya badzra zhes pa yang snang / 'gos kyi stong thun chen mor/ rgyal ba'i chos
la mnga' brnyes bdag

gi bla ma bzang po dpal/ zhes shrI bha dra bsgyur nas der bshad do/ /'di dang dges pa rdo rje bka' babs bzhi'i nang tshan gyi nag po dam tshig rdo rje gnyis gcig yin no/ /de
ltar rgyal sras sa 'dres pa sras kyi thu bo lnga dang bcas pa bzhugs pa'i skabs su de tsam na rgya gar 'phags yul du 'dus pa shin tu dar bar gyur te/ theg chen gyi paNDi
ta phal cher 'dus pa slob/ 'dus pa la nyams bzhes mdzad pa mang bar bshad pa yin la/ yang rdo rje 'chang dngos kyis sa bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rin chen la
gsang ba 'dus pa'i gdams pa stsal/ des sa ra ha dang klu sgrub gnyis la gdams/ klu sgrub kyis ma taM gi pa/ de nas tai lo pa nA ro pa sogs brgyud pa'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i
chos skor gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir dar ba'i nang tshan mar lugs grub thob nang brgyud du grags pa yang deng sang gi bar du bzhugs te/ de yang byang chub sems dpa' blo gros
rin chen zhes bya ba 'di ni/ mdo lugs ltar na dge bsnyen chen po li tsa bI dri ma med par grags pa ste/ 'di'i lo rgyus ni lan cig dge bsnyen chen po 'dis mal chen po bcas
nas bsnyun tshul bstan pa la/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis bsnyun 'dri bar ma spobs/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'phags pa 'jam dpal la khyod
shes rab kyi spobs pa dang ldan pas dge bsnyen chen po'i bsnyun dris shig gsungs pas/ der 'jam dpal gyis dge bsnyen chen po ji tsam nas bsnyun dris pas/ 'khor ba thog
ma med pa nas gsungs

te/ de ni 'khor ba thog ma med pa la dgongs so/ /yang ji tsam na dwangs par 'gyur gsungs pas/ 'khor ba ma stong gi bar du nad las mi thar gsungs/ de ni 'khor ba la tha ma med
pa la dgongs so/ /de nas yang 'jam dpal gyis yang dag pa'i don ji lta bu lags zhus pas ci yang mi gsungs/ lan gnyis lan gsum gyi bar du dris pas kyang ci yang mi gsungs
so/ /de ni don dam smra bsam brjod du med pa la dgongs te/ rgyal ba'i sras po cang mi gsungs/ /mi gsungs pas ni rgya cher bshad/ /ces gsungs pa'i don yin no/ /de lta bu'i
dge bsnyen chen po de gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa ltar na blo gros rin chen zhes bya ba sa bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshul bzung ba zab mo'i don thugs su chud pa
mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa che ba'i yon tan dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa zhig yin te 'dir mdo tsam mo/ /de lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po dga' ldan gyi
lha'i bu blo gros rin chen gyis 'dzam bu'i gling du gsang ba 'dus pa'i gdams pa sbyin pa'i gdul bya yod dam med snyam du dgongs nas gzigs pas/ sa ra ha dang klu sgrub gnyis
snod ldan du gzigs nas de gnyis la gdams/ de gnyis kyi nang nas klu sgrub kyis ma taM gi pa la gnang / des grub chen tai lo pa la stsal pa yin te/ de yang tai lo pa ni
dang po rab tu byung / de nas rje btsun mas byin gyis brlabs te sngags dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i don phyin ci ma log par rtogs shing / de nas klu sgrub 'tshol du phyin
pas/

bla ma mtshan gsang ba ste ma taM gi pa spyil po na bzhugs pa dang mjal te/ klu sgrub gang na yod dris pas/ slob dpon dri za'i yul du chos ston du byon gsungs/ khyod rjes su
'dzin par nga btang pa yin gsungs pa dang / der tai lo pas maNDal phul rjes su 'dzin par zhu zhes zhus pas/ dpal gsang pa 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur/ sems kyi
de kho na nyid ngo sprad nas ma brjed par sgoms shig gsungs/ de nas da khyod shar phyogs bhaM ga la'i rgyud ha ri ka la zhes bya bar za hor gyi grong khyer yod pas/ de nyid
sprul pa'i rgyal po ud ma skye zhes bya bas byin gyis brlabs pas bsgrub thag nye ba'i gnas yin pas der song la/ grong khyer de'i dbus na panytsa pa ta na zhes pa'i tshong
'dus yod/ de nas bha ri smad 'tshong ma 'khor mang po dang bcas pa yod pas/ de'i g.yog gyis la lam gyi rtogs pa sbyongs shig ring po mi thogs par phyag rgya chen po
mchog gi dngos grub thob nas 'gro ba mang po'i don byed par 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan to/ /de nas tai lo pas de bzhin mdzad pas grub pa brnyes nas nam mkha' la rang dgar bzhugs
pa la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul mang du bstan pas/ mi rnams ngo mtshar skyes/ bha ri mos g.yog tu bkol ba la 'gyod pa skyes te phyag phul rjes su gzung bar zhu zhus te/
mo'i rgyud byin gyis brlabs pas des kyang grub pa thob bo/ /tshul de rgyal pos thos nas ngo mtshar skyes te/ rgyal po 'khor bcas slob dpon gyi zhal blta bar 'ongs pa la/
slob dpon gyis nam mkhar bzhugs nas til mar gyi dpes mtshon pa'i /

gdams pa zab mo gsungs pas/ rgyal po 'khor bcas grub pa thob ste mkha' spyod du bzhud pas re zhig yul phyogs de stong par gyur to/ /de lta bu'i slob dpon des ye shes kyi mkha'
'gro ma las chos dngos su nyan nus/ 'og min du rdo rje 'chang chen po las kyang dngos su gdams pa nod pa yin la/ de dag kyang dag pa'i snang ba kho nas mjal ba yin te/
grub chen nyid kyi gsung las/ ngas ni sangs rgyas stong dag la/ /bsnyen bkur yang dag ngas kyang byas/ /sa rab dga' ba ngas kyang thob/ /sprul pa bye ba phrag brgya yis/
/klu sgrub ArYa de wa dang / /bcom ldan 'das dang ngas gtam byas/ /nga rang bde ba can du 'gro/ /zhes kyang gsungs pa yin no/ /de nas mthar mkha' spyod du gshegs so/ /de
nyid kyis rjes su bzung zhing byin gyis brlabs pa ni jo bo nA ro ta pa ste/ 'di ni yul kha che ba yin pa las/ dur khrod chen po gcig tu phyin nas bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i
bsten pa thon tsam na sa g.yos chen po byung ba na/ re zhig nas rnal 'byor ma sngon mo gnyis byung nas/ khyod shar phyogs pa tai lo pa'i rigs yin pas shar phyogs su song
zhig zer/ khyed su yin dris pas/ slob dpon klu'i sring mo yin zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de gang na bzhugs kyang 'dri ma nus snyam 'gyod bzhin pas shar phyogs su
phyin pas/ gan dha bu ri'i gtsug lag khang du rnal 'byor pa ras nag po'i angga rag gon pa/ mig rtsa dmar zhing / so dung so 'khor mar yod pa/ dar dmar po'i cod pan bcings
/

pa gcig gis nya gson po spar mo gang khyer byung ste/ dge 'dun gyi 'bras kyi tsha ba g.yos pa'i me la blugs so/ /de la dge 'dun ma mnyes par ngan pa 'di la rgyob zer ba na/
rnal 'byor pa des khyed rnams mi dga' na/ song song gsungs nas se gol gtogs gtogs mdzad pas/ nya tsho mkha' la 'khyug 'khyug song ba dang / dge 'dun rnams kyis grub thob
yin par shes nas bzod par gsol nas mchod gnas su bzhugs par zhus pas ma gnang ngo / /de phyir byon tsa na/ nA ro pa'i bsam pa la tai lo pa yin nam snyam nas phyag dang bskor
ba byas/ zhabs spyi bor blangs te/ bdag la mkha' 'gro'i lung bstan pa lags pas rjes su gzung bar zhu zhus pas/ nA ro pa'i thugs kar rdog pa cig bzhag nas cang mi gsungs
bar bzhud do/ /nA ro pas kyang phyi bzhin 'brangs pas/ lha khang thog bcu gsum yod pa gcig gi steng du byon nas/ 'jig rten gsum na bla ma'i bka' dang mi 'gal ba byed
pa yod na/ 'di na mar mchongs nus pa su yod gsungs/ der nA ro pa'i thugs la mi gzhan ni mi 'dug nga la zer ba yin nam snyam nas/ lha khang kha nas mchongs pas/ rus pa chag
nas gsus pa la zug ste na tsha tshugs pa med pa byung ba nas/ bla ma byon nas khyod na'am gsungs/ na lags ro bzhin thal lo zhus pas na ro zhes grags so zhes gser sdings
pas mdzad pa'i gsang 'dus bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge las byung mod/ nA ro pa'i sgra don de ltar du 'chad pa ni nor ba ste/ bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi /

tas rab dbye las/ dka' ba spyad pas a na na/ /ro ru song zhes 'chad pa dang / /zhes gsungs pas so/ /des na nA ro zhes pa ni 'phags yul na bram ze'i rigs bcu drug yod pa'i nang
nas rigs bzang shos nA ro ta pa zhes bya ba'i rigs yin pas na nA ro ta pa zhes bya ba yin par bshad pa ni 'thad ldan yin no/ /de nas bla mas phyag gis yul yul mdzad nas
phu phaTa? sos par gyur cig gsungs pas sngar bzhin sos so/ /yang dus gcig gi tshe tai lo pas me tog cig bsdus nas nA ro pa la gtad de/ da lta 'di na mar la bag ma gcig
'ong bas/ me tog 'di mgo la thogs la nu ma mnyes shig gsungs shing / tai lo pa rang bzhud song ba dang / dum tsam nas bag ma de byung ba la nA ro pas tai lo pa ji skad gsungs
pa bzhin byas pas/ gnya' 'o rnams kyi brdungs te shi la thug pa na/ tai lo pa byon nas sngar bzhin byin rlabs mdzad pas gsos/ yang lan gcig tai lo pa nags khrod cig
na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ nA ro pas bsod snyoms la phyin pas dge 'dun la ston mo byed pa dang 'phrad de/ tsha ba bslangs pas ro mchog dang ldan pa zhig 'dug pas/ tai lo pa la
drang dgos snyam ste khyer 'ongs nas zhus pas/ zhim zhim ltar legs par gsol te zhal nas nA ro pa tshod ma zhim gsungs/ nA ro pa'i thugs la sngar nas ci phul kyang dgyes
pa'i bzhed med pa la/ da res dges par 'dug snyam nas slar slong du phyin pas/ ma byin pa dang / nA ro pas phru ba khyer te bros pas/ dge 'dun rnams kyis bdas pas zin /

nas brdungs pas shi la khad pa la sngar bzhin byin rlabs mdzad pas nad las grol lo/ /gzhan yang mkha' khung du smyug tshal brgyab pa dang / nam phyed zas slong gsungs nas bslang
pas brdungs pa dang / lus kyis tai lo pa bzhud pa'i zam pa byas pas srin bus zos pa dang / tsandan gyi me la mchongs su bcug pa dang / thang chen po la ngal ma gsos
par rbab khur gsungs pa la khur ba dang / rgyal po'i chung ma dang lhan cig sdod cig gsungs pa la brdungs pa dang / blon po'i chung ma dang lhan cig sdod cig gsungs pa la
bsdad pas brdungs pa dang / nga'i rig ma dang lhan cig sdod cig gsungs pa la bsdad pas mes bsregs pa dang / khrag gi maNDal la sha'i tshom bu bkod de phul gsungs pa la
de bzhin mdzad pa dang / nA ro pa'i phyag rgya ma la byas pas mtshan ma langs pa rdos brdungs pa la sogs pa mdor na nA ro pas tai lo pa lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du bsten dka'
ba chen po bcu bzhi dang du blangs te ji skad gsungs pa bzhin bsgrubs so/ /de ltar gser sdings bas mdzad pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar las dka' spyad mang du mdzad pa'i
dang po gsum la bum dbang sogs dbang dang po gsum thob tshul sbyar nas/ slar de ltar na nA ro pas lo bcu gnyis su zhabs tog byas pas chos ci yang ma zhus pas/ da zhu
dgos snyam nas phyag dang bskor ba byas maNDal phul nas zhabs spyi bor blangs te yang dag pa'i gdams ngag zhus pas/ spyan phyogs bzhir gzigs te/ mchil lham phud nas gcu gcu
ba cig dpral /

bar brgyab nas bde ba chen por brgyal lo/ /brgyal ba sangs tsa na theg pa mtha' dag gi chos thugs la shar te mi shes pa gang yang mi 'dug go /de'i dus su a thung skye ba med
pa'i gdams ngag gnang ste/ mi mno/ mi bsam/ mi dpyad/ sems rang bzhin gyi gnas par zhog gsungs/ yang zhus pas/ bsam pa'i yul las 'das/ brjod pa'i tshig las 'das/ mtshon
pa'i dpe las 'das/ tai lo pas ci yang bstan du med gsungs so/ /de ltar dka' spyad bcu bzhi po de re re la'ang mnyes tshor khyad par can re skyes shing sa bcu bzhi bgrod
pa yin no zhes gsungs pa ni ma 'brel te/ dka' spyad dang po gsum dang bum dbang sogs sbyar bas dbang thob par bstan/ lo bcu gnyis su zhabs tog byas chos ci yang ma zhus zhes
bshad pa ni dbang chos ma yin par gsung rgyur snang ba/ de ltar na gsang sngags kyi chos sam lam gyi rtsa ba dbang bskur nyid yin par rgyud sde thams cad las bsngags
brjod dang bcas gsung par mi 'thad par 'gyur zhing / dka' spyad bcu bzhis sa bcu bzhi bgrod ces pa yang nor te/ sa bcu gsum zhes pa'i tha snyad gsungs kyis/ rdo rje theg
pa'i lugs kyi sa bcu bzhi sogs su bshad pa ni sa btags pa pa'am/ 'thad ldan ma yin no/ /yang gser sding pas mdzad pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus las/ de nas nA ro pas bla
ma drin che bas drin lan zhig mdzad par dgongs nas byon pa na/ mgar ba'i gling du grogs po mgar ba gcig yod pa'i sar bzhag nas//

srod la lo rgyus ngo mtshar gyi gtam la yengs/ de nas gnyid bzi song tsam na/ gnyid sad sad pa dang mgar ba la tug gi re mos yod pa dang / nam langs snyam ste tho tug byas
pas thams cad tug gi song bas/ der slob dpon so ma sod zhe sdang skyes pas/ de cis lan bsam pas tug gis lan par 'dug tug de gang nas byung bsam pas mgar ba'i khyim nas byung
/ de nas tug thams cad song 'dug dpe de bzhin du ngas zhe sdang ngam so ma sod pa de rang gi sems las byung / sems stong pa nyid las byung / stong pa de chos sku skye
med go ba'i brda byung ste/ de yang bla ma'i drin yin snyam ste mos gus lhag par skyes nas/ bye ru bre do tsam btsal nas bla ma la 'bul du phyin pas/ tai lo pa'i thugs la
nA ro pa 'di da rung rnal 'byor pa chen por mi 'dug snyam nas/ bye ma'i sgang bu zhig bye rur byin gyis brlabs nas de'i steng du bzhugs pas/ nA ro pa'i thugs la bla ma
la bye ru dgos pa mi 'dug bla ma rang 'dod na sa gzhi'ang bye rur bsgyur du 'dug pa la snyam nas/ bla ma'i phyogs su bye ru gtor nas btang ngo / /de nas chos bshad pa gal
che'am bsgom pa gal che bla ma la zhus pas/ thod pa dri chen gyis gang ba la mi'i rtsib mas khyem bu byas nas gsol te/ de nas nA ro pa la byin pas bltas pas mdog mi sdug
bsnams pas dri mi zhim par 'dug 'on kyang zo zhig bya ba'i brda yin snyam nas zos pas ro mchog brgya dang ldan par 'dug nas/ der bshad pa gtso bor byed pa ni mi gtsang ba'i
/

kha dog dang dri dang 'dra bar 'dug bsgrub pa gtsor byed pa ni mi gtsang ba'i ro zhib pa dang 'dra ste/ nyon mongs pa ye shes su 'char bar 'dug snyam pa dang / bla ma'i zhal
nas de tsug yin gsungs te dbang bzhi lam du byed pa'i brda yin no zhes gsungs pas/ lo rgyus de la yang nang 'gal cung zad 'dug ste yi ges 'jigs nas btang snyoms bzhag go
/'o na dka' spyad rnams ma rdzogs gong gdams ngag cung zad kyang ma bstan nam snyam na/ lo rgyus tshad ldan rnams las/ dka' spyad ma rdzogs bar gdams pa ma bstan par/ slar
bstan pa kho na 'byung bas/ tshul de bzhin du bshad na/ gong du bstan pa ltar dka' spyad mang po zhig dang du blangs nas/ yang nA ro pas tai lo pa'i phyi bzhin du 'brangs
nas thang stong zhig tu slebs pa na/ tai lo pa cung zhig mnyam par bzhag nas/ nA ro pa la khyod yun ring por tsha grang la sogs pa gang yang yid la mi byed par dka'
ba don du gnyer ba ci 'dod pa yin gsungs pa la/ nA ro pas kho bo ni yang dag pa'i gdams ngag 'dod do zhus pas/ 'o na maNDal gyis gsungs pa la/ chu med zhus pas/ dri chus
gyis gsungs nas/ de bzhin mdzad nas maNDal gyi me tog bkram pa dang / slob dpon gyis maNDal gyi 'jim pa cig blangs nas/ nA ro pa'i zhal la brgyab pas mi rtog pa skyes te/
de yang lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes mtshon par byed pa'i phyir byin gyis brlabs par mdzad pa yin no/ /de nas dang por dbang dang / phyis su rgyud dang //

gdams ngag ma lus pa gnang ba las/ thog mar bskyed pa'i rim pa dang / gzhi 'khor ba'i gnad rtsa dang rlung dang byang chub kyi sems la sogs pa mtshon byed thams cad bstan nas/
mtshon bya don zhus pas/ tai lo pa'i zhal nas/ kye ho 'di ni rang rig ye shes te/ /ngag gi lam 'das spyod yul min/ /tai lo pa yis ci yin bstan du med/ /rang la rang gis
bslan te shes par byos/ /zhes gsungs nas rgya mtsho dang 'dra ba'i mtshon bya don bstan te/ da khyod paNDi ta'i chas ma 'dzin par rnal 'byor pa'i cha lugs kyis sgrub pa
snying por gyis shig skye ba 'dir mchog gi dngos grub thob par 'gyur ro zhes dam tshig phog nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas nA ro pas me tog 'phrog pa'i lha khang zhes
bya ba'i byang phyogs grong khyer chung ngu zhig yod pa na rgan mo gcig gis 'tsho ba phul nas bsgrub pa snying por mdzad kyin bzhugs pa na/ dus re zhig na mu stegs gcer
bu pa rnams rtsod pa rgyal nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa 'jig par nye ba na/ rgyal pos paNDi ta lnga brgya bsags te me tog gi phreng ba gtad pas sus kyang len ma nus par/
rgyal po na re/ da dung bgros la rtsod pa gyis shig gal te mi nus na gtsug lag khang gcer bu pa la 'bul lo byas pas/ paNDi ta rnams gros byed pa'i tshe/ rgan mo zhig na
re/ nga'i khyim na nA ro pa bzhugs zer ba dang / der dge 'dun gyis gsol ba btab pas sngar tai lo pa'i gsung ma dran par zhal gyis bzhes so/ /der gcer bu pa 'ong du ma btub
pa la/ kho'i lha khang gi gam du/ rgol ba phyir rgol gnyis//

dpang po rgyal po dang gsum gyi khri bshams te rtsod pa byas pas slob dpon zhan zhan 'dra nas/ thugs la nga lta bu'i smra ba'i dbang phyug zhan pa ltar 'dug pa ci yin snyam
du bsam pas/ sngar slob dpon tai lo pa'i gsung yod pa de bcag pa'i nyes pa dran nas bzod gsol byas te yid kyis gsol ba btab pas tai lo pa'i phyag g.yon par mi'i thod pa
bcad ma khad cig thogs nas byon pa la/ nA ro pas phyag 'tshal bas/ snying rje dang bral ba srin po'i gzugs can 'di lta bu la phyag 'tshal ba de nyid kyi pham pa'i gnas su
gyur to zer ba la/ ti lo pas pham pham zhes gsungs nas/ kho'i lha khang mchod rten gyi gzugs 'dra ba zur brgyad dang gsum thog yod pa la sdigs mdzub lan gsum mdzad pas thog
gsum ka 'gyel bas gcer bu ba rnams skrag te thams cad kyis slob dpon gyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal gcer bu pa rnams sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la btsud do/ /de nas tai lo pas
nA ro pa la/ da khyod kyis skye ba 'di la mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i skal ba med kyi/ chos ston cig 'gro ba mang po la phan/ khyod bas kyang slob ma dang / de'i slob
ma nas mar rim pa bzhin du phan je cher 'gyur la/ bar dor phyag rgya chen po 'grub par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas nA ro pas bshad sgrub gnyis
ka mdzad pas rtogs pa 'khrungs nas/ 'char ba med cing nub pa med/ /nyin mo med cing mtshan mo'ang med/ /ces sogs kyi rtogs brjod kyi glu yang gsungs so/ /de lta bu'i /
jo bo nA ro ta pas phyag rgya chen /

po mchog gi dngos grub dus der ma thob kyang / rgyal po dpung dang bcas pa rengs par byed pa dang / tshogs 'khor gyi dus su ni shing tog la sogs pa dgug nus pa dang / sbyin
sreg gi tshe thab kyi nang du lha sum cu rtsa gnyis zhal blta nus pa la sogs pa ting nge 'dzin gyi rtogs pa brtan par thob pas/ pur sbyangs pa'i shul du yang zla ba re re
bzhin rol mo'i sgra dang / me tog gi char la sogs pa'i lha'i mchod pa yang kun gyis mthong zhing thos pa yin no/ /de dag ni 'phags yul du 'phags lugs kyi bla ma brgyud
pa ji ltar byon pa'i tshul bstan zin pa yin la/ gnyis pa ye shes zhabs lugs pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas ye shes zhabs lugs 'phags yul du dar tshul
ni/ mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang dbyer med pa'i/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs la gnang ba yin te/ de yang slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyis
spyir gsang ba 'dus pa paNDi ta nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam la gtugs nas zhus shing / khyad par slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis dngos su byin gyis brlabs yin te/ de yang
slob dpon 'dis thog mar slob dpon seng ge bzang po la pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhung lugs bslabs te/ yon tan bshes gnyen la sogs pa'i rigs ldan rnams la 'chad rtsod rtsom
gsum gyi sgo nas dar bar mdzad/ phyis nub phyogs o rgyan du byon nas slob dpon 'jol sgeg rdo rje la gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan cing / yang
yul de nyid du lcam /

legs smin dang / gu ni ni zhes bya ba'i bla ma zhig la yang gsang 'dus mang du gsan no/ /yang yul dza lan nA thar slob dpon ba mo la tsam pa ta bya ba la yang gsang ba 'dus
pa'i chos skor legs par gsan nas lho phyogs kyi yul du/ slob dpon ba liM ta A tsArYa zhes bya ba mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba'i bla ma lo dgu'i
bar zas gos dang longs spyod kyis mnyes par byas nas gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud bco brgyad gsan pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas khyod kyis don ma rtogs gsungs pa na/ slob dpon
gyi thugs dgongs la don ma rtogs na rtogs pa mi skye dgongs nas/ rdo rje gdan gyi byang phyogs u pa tha zhes pa stag dang dom la sogs pa gcan gzan ma rungs pa gnas pa'i yul
du rgyud kyi glegs bam mgul du btags nas zla ba drug sgrub pa mdzad pas/ ston zla ra ba'i skar ma rgyal gyi nub skya rengs shar ba tsam na sprul pa'i dge slong bla ma
gnyis 'jol sgeg rdo rje 'jam rdor dang bcas pa'i zhal mngon sum du gzigs te/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i zhal nas 'jam dpal zhal lung du grags pa'i rdzogs rim lung bstan dang bcas
pa gnang ba la brten nas 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor 'di'i srol rgya cher btod pa yin la/ slob dpon de la slob ma'i tshogs kyang mthong ba'i chos la mya
ngan las 'das pa'i gang zag bzhi/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad bka' 'dzin par nus nges shes pa'i grwa pa bco brgyad/ de rnams kyi nang du rtsa rgyud rgyud phyi ma dang bcas
pa la 'grel pa byed mkhan bcu gsum tsam byung zhing / de'i /

nang nas mar me mdzad bzang pos gsang ba 'dus pa lha bcu dgu'i dkyil chog mdzad/ mar me mdzad kyis 'jam dpal bshes gnyen bya ba'i slob dpon gcig dang / dpal sde gnyis la gsungs/
phyi mas bi ma la gupta ste dri med sbas pa la gnang / de nas rin chen rdo rje/ ratna kirti ste rin chen grags pa bla ma pandha pa'i bar du rim par byon pa'i brgyud
rim gcig dang / yang mar me mdzad nas kun dga' snying po/ tha ga na zhi ba/ dad byed go cha/ padmA ka ra zhes bya ba'i bar brgyud pa dang / mar me mdzad kyi slob ma 'jam
dpal grags pa nas/ dpal sde/ dri med sbas pa/ yi ge pa/ nag po pa/ ye shes dpal/ ba liM ta A tsArYa ste bod skad du gtor ma'i slob dpon zhes pa la brgyud pa dang / yang
rin chen grags pa nas sa manta bha tra ste kun tu bzang po/ dznyA na shrI mi tra ste ye shes dpal gyi bshes gnyen/ ratna kIrti ste dkon mchog grags pa/ puNye shrI ste bsod
nams dpal gyi bar du brgyud pa ste 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i brgyud rim la yang brgyud tshul mang du byung ba yin no/ /de rnams kyis 'phags yul du byon pa'i gsang
ba 'dus pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas 'dus pa 'phags yul du ji ltar dar ba'i tshul bstan zin nas/ gnyis pa bod yul du byon pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i
rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas bod yul du ji ltar dar ba'i tshul la yang 'phags skor gyi brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas gtso bor 'phags lugs nyid ji ltar dar ba'i
tshul dang / ye shes zhabs /

lugs sogs kyi brgyud rim bstan pa'i sgo nas lugs gzhan dar tshul dang / dang po la yang 'gos lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas lugs de ji ltar dar ba'i
tshul dang / mar lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas lugs de nyid ji ltar dar ba'i tshul dang / sa lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i
sgo nas sa lugs ji ltar dar ba'i tshul dang gsum las/ dang po ni/ 'gos lo tsA ba bsod nams rtse mo zhes bya ba de nyid kyi sku drin las dar zhing de nyid nas brgyud pa
ste/ de yang mgon po 'di 'khrungs pa'i yul ni rta nag yin zhing / slob dpon 'gos kyi ris yin pas so/ /yab yum gnyis ming sring yin pa 'dus pa'i sras yin pas na khug pa/ ming
sring bsnal ba la ngo tsha nas rta nag phu'i lhas shig tu btsar phyin nas lhas su btsas pas lhas btsas zhes grags pa yin par bshad/ yang bu ston rin po ches yab yum gnyis
ka 'gos yin pas na khug pa dang / lhas phug tu 'khrungs pas na lhas btsas su grags pa yin gsungs la/ gang ltar de lta bu'i 'gos lo des gzhon nu'i dus su zur pa la rnying
ma slob par byon pas/ der chos ma bslabs par yang yang mnar ba zhig byung ba na yid 'byung ste/ ngas rgya gar du phyin la khyed rnams la lan zhig bya'i gsungs nas/ gyi
jo zla ba'i 'od zer dang 'grogs nas rgya gar du byon pas/ shAnti pa dang dpal sbas gnyis grongs nas mi bzhugs/ gzhan sa 'dres pa'i slob ma gsum bzhugs pa'i /

dus su 'byor te/ de'i skabs na 'phags yul na paNDi ta mnyam po la/ 'dus pa la mkhas pa rnams gral mgor 'jog cing / chos 'dus pa la kha zin che bar 'dug nas thog mar 'dus pa
slob dgos dgongs te/ gsang ba 'dus pa la su mkhas dris pas/ sa 'dres pa'i slob ma rnams mkhas zer bas/ mngon shes can/ btsun mo can rnams la 'dus pa'i chos skor gsan/ bslab
sbyong yang 'dus pa la mdzad nas bod du byon/ de dus khams nas mar ston seng rgyal byon/ 'gos lo la chos mang du zhus/ zang zing gi dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab pas mnyes
par byas/ slar yang 'gos kyis rgya gar du byon/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje la 'dus pa'i chos skor gsan/ de ltar paNDi ta mngon shes can/ btsun mo can/ nag po dam tshig
rdo rje dang gsum la gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor mthil phyin par gsan nas bla ma gsum po de dag gi gsung bgros rnams so sor zin bris su 'bri bar mdzad pa la 'gos kyi shog
ril gsum du grags/ gzhan yang rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paNDi ta sprin gyi shugs can la yang 'dus pa gsan pas/ 'gos kyi gsang 'dus gsan pa'i bla ma bzhi yin la/ 'ga' zhig
las 'gos kyi gsang 'dus gsan pa'i bla ma gsum las ma bshad kyang / phyi ma 'di la yang gsan par 'gos lo nyid kyis rgyud kyi mchan chen gyi mjug tu bshad pas rtsod pa med/
'on kyang gsang ba 'dus pa rim lnga'i khrid ni dang po gsum kho na las gsan par nges so/ /spyir lo chen 'dis 'phags yul du lan gsum byon/ gong gi /

bla ma bzhi po de'i steng du kha che khri brtan gyi tsandra ha ri/ bal po rdzong gi nA ga ko Ti/ bal po mthil gyi tsa huM ngu dang / sa ra ba bya ba rnams la sogs pa mi'i bla
ma bdun cu/ mkha' 'gro ma gnyis te bdun cu rtsa gnyis te bdun cu rtsa gnyis bsten te mdo sngags kyi chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan/ chos dang chos min gyi rnam
dbye legs par phye ba'i bstan bcos sngags log sun 'byin bya ba mdzad/ khyad par gsang ba 'dus pa la rtsa rgyud kyi tshig 'grel mchan chen dang / don 'grel stong thun chen
mo sogs mdzad de 'dus pa'i bstan pa nyi ma shar ba ltar mdzad pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i 'gos kyi gsang 'dus gsan pa'i bla ma bzhi'i nang gi sprin gyi shugs can dang ga ya
dha ra gnyis gcig yin par/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rgyun zin bris 'ga' zhig las bshad/ bu ston rin po ches rgya gar shar phyogs su rgyal po sprin gyi shugs can zhes bshad
do/ /gang ltar 'gos lo 'dis rgya gar du yang lan gsum byon par paN chen nyi zla seng ge'i rnam bshad las bshad/ bu ston rin po ches ni bcu gnyis byon par bshad kyang
/ de ni yi ge ma dag gam snyam mo/ /gang ltar 'gos la slob ma yang rgyud kyi ka ba tshugs pa bzhi/ man ngag gi gdung ma theg pa brgyad/ las tshogs dang 'phrin las la mkhas
pa rnams lcam dang gral ma gshibs pa ltar mang du byung ba yin pa las/ ka chen bzhi ni mar ston seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rlan grags dbang / sum ston me 'bar/ mi nyag dharmA
tsandra /

dang bzhi yin la/ yang bu ston rin po che'i bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed las/ dharmA tsandra dang rlan ma bgrangs par/ shangs kyi bab ston byang chub rgyal mtshan/ gnyal
gyi gshong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang gnyis po 'dren par mdzad la/ gdung ma brgyad ni 'byed kyi rdog ston chen po/ rong gi brang ti rgyal po/ rta nag gi mkhas pa bsod
rgyal la sogs pa'o zhes gsungs nas ka chen bzhi la 'dren tshul mi mthun pa cung zad tsam byung / gdung ma bzhi ltar na rdog dge ser/ dbus pa dbang 'bum/ lho pa rdo rje
snying po/ gnyal pa chos kyi shes rab dang bzhi/ brgyad ltar na rdog ston chen po sogs brgyad la ngos 'dzin dgos kyang / brgyad kyi ngos 'dzin gsal kha can bgrangs pa zhig
ma byung bas btsal dgos so/ /de lta bu'i 'gos kyi slob ma rnams kyi nang nas mar ston seng rgyal ni/ 'jed so rong bya bar sku 'khrungs/ 'dis rje btsun 'gos kyi snyan pa
gsan nas/ de'i drung du byon dbang dang gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa mtha' dag nos te/ 'gos lo la rin po che'i gser 'bum dang / rta nag po seng ge srab med bya ba zhig
dang / seng ldeng gi sga dngul gyi shan pa brgyab pa zhig sogs kyis thog drangs brgya 'bul mdzad de/ zang zing gi 'bul nod kyis mnyes par byas/ de nas 'jed kyis so rong
du dgon pa ram sding btab ste/ de'i gnas bdag tu bsam yas kyi chos skyong gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po tsi'u dmar po spyan drangs nas bskos/ de nyid la gdung ma bzhi'am brgyad
kyi nang tshan rdog chen po ye shes seng ge zhes bya bas gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags /

skor phal che ba gsan cing / khyad par 'gos lo chen po la yongs su rdzogs par gsan nas dar bar mdzad pa la phyis su 'dus pa rngog lugs su grags pa yin te/ de yang rngog ye
shes seng ge de'i sras nyi ma seng ge de'i gcung po dbu mar ra/ de'i dbon po rdor sems dang bzhis khams nas 'ongs nas rta nag sgro mon can du babs/ 'gos kyis rgya gar sngon
ma 'khor ba dang mjal nas/ 'gos lo chen po la gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang zhus/ rgyud mnyan/ man ngag la nan tan cher mdzad pas/ man ngag gi gdung ma theg
par grags so/ /de nas dbu ma ra dang rdor seng gnyis kyis srin po rir 'dul ba bslabs te/ slar dbu ma ras 'jed gad phung bzung / rdor seng gis sdong khrod bzung / rngog ye
shes seng ges 'jed dga' ldan dang / dol du me tog mdzes ldan bya ba'i dgon pa gnyis btab/ de nas phyis mar ston seng ge rgyal mtshan la 'dus pa'i rgyud 'grel chen po'i nan
tan mdzad/ 'gos kyi phyi 'gyur gyi gsang sngags kyi chos rnams la mkhas/ mar ston gyis kyang dgon pa ram sdings gtad pa bzung ngo / /de nyid la rang gi sras nyi ma seng
ge'i spyir chos mang po dang / yab chos gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor ma lus pa gsan zhing / dbu tshad la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid thams cad dang / gsang sngags kyi chos phal cher
la sbyangs pas shin tu mkhas pa thub pa dang 'dra bas rngog mu nir grags so/ /des dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gcig la brag ltag gi dgon pa btab/ nyi shu rtsa gsum la dzambha

la'i bsgrub pa mdzad pas zhag dus la rtags gang yang ma byung bar thugs mug ste/ dzambha la'i rdo sku 'phangs par brtsams pas/ gzod zhal bstan gsung byon nas bla ma 'di chos
mkhas shing longs spyod kyang che bas slob ma che btsun dpag tu med pa 'dus shing / khyad par dbus gtsang gi jo sras mi bzhir grags pa byung ste/ 'grig 'tshams kyi zhang
/ kha rag gi gnyos/ sman lung gi dpyal/ yar lung gi khu rnams kyi bla mar gyur/ gzhan yang lo shAkya seng ge rlan btsad tsha nyi ma lcam sku mched la sogs pa bu chen mang
du byung nas thams cad kyi bkur sti'i gnas su gyur to/ /de la zur du sras zhig byung ba gzhan gyis ma tshor bar byas khams su btang / cung zad cher skyes pa na yab gshegs
pa'i gdan sar su bkod zer bgros byas pa na 'ga' zhig na re/ mdo khams na bla ma'i sras yod zer nas gdan drangs slob gnyer byed du bcug pas/ nga'i yab chos gang yin zer/
'dus pa yin byas pas/ de la su mkhas zer ba la/ khye re lha khang pa mkhas zer nas/ der byon gsung gleng mdzad pas/ nged ye shes zhabs lugs pa yin/ khyod kyi yab chos
'phags lugs yin pas/ rlan btsad tsha nyi ma lcam can du byon zer nas/ de'i drung du byon 'dus pa yongs su rdzogs pa zhus/ slar bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyi zhabs la gtugs
te sa skya pa'i chos mang po yang gsan/ sa skyar 'dus pa'i 'chad nyan yang rgya cher mdzad la/ khong pa thag ring pas lam bteg la bya ru gzhung gnang bas zhang bya ru bar
grags/

mtshan dngos rdog ArYa de wa zhes bya ba yin la/ 'di gong du 'gos rngog pa'i bla ma gong ba rnams sgrub thabs kyi bshad pa rgyun du mdzad pas bskyed rim bsgom pa zhar la 'byung
bas dkyil chog brtsams pa yang med cing / rim lnga'i khrid dmigs rgyun du so sor bsgom pa ma gtogs/ mang po tshogs nas sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i phyag srol yang med pa
la/ ArYa de wa sa paN gyi slob mar gyur phyin chad nas sa skya pa phyag len bde ba'i spyan zlos bzang po de khong gis rtogs nas/ 'dus pa'i dkyil chog dang / mchod 'phreng
sogs yig cha mang po mdzad nas gsang ba 'dus pa'i bsgrub mchod btsugs/ de'i dus su rdog ar de'i slob ma rnams kyi gsung bgros phyogs gcig tu bris pa bstod 'bum bya ba po
ti gcig dang / smad 'bum bya ba po ti gcig ste gsang 'dus kyi 'grel pa chen po lta bu zhig kyang byung nas 'dus pa la lag len bshad pa dang bcas pa shin tu dar bar mdzad
do/ /de lta bu'i rdog ArYa de wa la spyi mkhar 'jug gres ka'i rtag pa rin grags dang / rong lha steng gi gtsang smra seng dang / cha dkar mon mo brag gi mi nyag rdo rje
grags gsum gyis gsan/ yang rdog nyi ma seng ge la gzhu'i phug ka phug ston shes rab grags kyis gsan/ de nyid la'ang mi nyag rdo rje grags dang gtsang smra seng gnyis kyis
zhus/ de gnyis ka la lce ston mdo sde seng ges gsan/ yang rlan btsad tsha la rgya mkhar thang spe ba'i mkhan po 'phags pa skyabs kyis gsan pa yin te/ de yang thang spe mkhan
po 'phags pa skyabs ni gzhon nu la rab tu

byung nas/ dang por sa gzhi dmar por song song slob gnyer mdzad/ de nas bskyed rdzogs kyi don thugs nyams su bzhes pas nyams dang rtogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud
la 'khrungs shing 'gro don mang du mdzad nas sku gshegs pa'i tshe/ gzims khang la 'ja'i gdugs sum rim dang / gzhan yang 'ja' 'od kyis bar snang thams cad khyab pa sogs ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba dang / pur sbyangs pas thugs ma tshig par byon zhing / gdung dang ring bsrel yang mang du byung bar bshad do/ /de nyid
la rgyang ro gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od kyis gsang ba 'dus pa mar lugs dang 'gos lugs gnyis char cha tshang bar gsan/ gser sdings pa 'di gsang ba 'dus pa la shin tu mkhas
shing man ngag gi rigs kyang mang du mdzad la/ de lta bu'i gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od dang / rdog ArYa de wa'i slob ma rtag pa rin grags/ lce ston mdo sde seng ge dang
gsum char la kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer gyis gsan/ de la lce blo ldan seng ges gsan zhing / de gnyis char la 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtshos gsan pa yin te/ de yang 'phags
pa 'od 'di 'khrungs pa'i yul ni nyang stod thu gu dang nye ba na la spe zhes bya ba zhig yod pa de nyid de/ gdung rje rigs yin la/ sngags 'chang sha stag byung ba'i brgyud
pa yab rje po rdo rje bya ba dang / yum ma gcig rje mo rgyal mtshan 'bum zhes bya ba gnyis la sras brgyad 'khrungs pa'i bla ma 'di chung shos yin zhing / gcen po rnams
chung nar ma son pa la 'das

nas ma sos par/ 'di nyid bla ma jo 'tsho ba bya ba zhig gis bu mo'i cha lugs su bsgyur/ bu mo'i ming btags nas gsos te/ cung zad cher skyes pa na 'bri klog bslabs nas/ dpon
spe gsar dpal 'bum bya ba'i drung du yi ge mkhas pa phul du phyin pa sbyangs/ de nas lan cig byis pa mang po phyugs 'tsho ba'i gral la byon pa'i skabs su nyal nas bzhugs
pa na nam mkha' la sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs brnyan dpag tu med pa gzigs te/ de'i rkyen gyis rlung sems dbu mar chud par yang grags shing / de nas yab
'das pa'i tshe ma na re/ khyod mi chos la spro na sa zin snga bar byed/ de min na mi gcig po chos kyi rgyu bya ba yin pas/ ji ltar legs bsam mno thongs/ btsun pa byas phyin
chad nas chos mgo thon pa zhig dgos zer ba na/ mi chos dang 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs rig nas rab tu byung bar zhal gyis bzhes nas/ dgung lo bco lnga lon par nye ba'i tshe
kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer la mkhan po dang / 'jam gsar dbon po 'jam dpal la slob dpon zhus nas rab byung mdzad de mtshan yang 'phags pa'i 'od du btags/ de nas dgyes rdor
gyi rgyud brtag gnyis dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i sde snod la gsan sbyong mdzad nas/ dgung lo bcu drug pa la brtag gnyis dang / bco brgyad pa la phar phyin bshad pas/
bla ma chos sku ba mnyes nas/ da khyod rang chos dang chos ma yin pa dang / rigs pa dang mi rigs pa'i rnam dbye tshul bzhin du 'byed shes pa la/

tshad ma rig pa la mkhas pa zhig dgos pas tshad ma slobs gsungs pa la/ khong pa'i thugs dgongs la/ ngas tshad ma kho nar ma zad dbus gtsang gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad
kyi drung du phyin la yon tan phyogs med du shes pa zhig bya/ de la brgyags phye khur nas phyin kyang theg pa yang dka'/ theg na'ang da lta 'khur rgyu yang cher med pas/
de bas brgyags phye lag las 'dzag pa zhig bya dgos dgongs nas/ snyems su dpon bal po dge 'dun can du byon/ khong la phyag 'tshal dar phul nas/ bdag la ri mo bslab dgos
byas pas/ khong gis chang btsags dang gang khyer byung ba na/ bdag chang mi 'thung byas pas/ khyed snying nas rang mi 'thung ba yin nam zer/ zhe nas mi 'thung ba lags byas
pas/ ja bskol nas drangs/ gzhan yang bsnyen bkur bzang po zhig mdzad nas/ ston pa khyed tshugs ka bzang ba 'di bzhin byed pa ngo mtshar che/ tshul 'di bzhin byed pa la
ri mo ma bslabs pa drag yon tan 'di mtha' ngan pa zhig 'dug pas/ ltogs rir shi ba gang byas kyang mi srid gsung nan chen pos ldog kyang / bdag la mno dgongs 'di 'dra zhig
bdog pas cis kyang slob dgos zhus pas/ dpon gyis kyang / khong gi gus pa'i spyod lam/ don gnyer gyi 'dun pa/ 'bad pa'i nan tan rnams la blo mgu nas/ man ngag yongs su rdzogs
pa gnang ste/ lo gcig la ri mo nan ltar legs pa zhig mkhyen nas/ dgung lo nyi shu bzhes pa'i tshe/ bla ma chos sku ba'i drung du rim lnga'i smar khrid zhus nas

bsgoms pas nyams rtags khyad par can 'khrungs/ de nas gsang 'dus rngog lugs dang / mar lugs gnyis ka'i bshad bka' dang / dus 'khor 'bro lugs kyi bshad pa rnams gsan zhing /
gtso cher gsang 'dus rngog lugs la sbyangs nas/ dgung lo nyer gsum pa la gsang 'dus la bshad pa mdzad/ de nas bla ma 'di dang ras pa nam mkha' rdo rje bya ba gnyis kyis
'gran nas yo ga la thugs sbyong mdzad cing / de dag gi bar la rdo rje 'byung ba'i dbang bka' dang bshad bka'/ de nyid snang ba'i stod 'grel gyi dbang bka' bshad bka'/ dpal
mchog stod 'grel gyi rigs bsdus dang / rdo rje sems dpa'i dbang bka' bshad bka'/ dpal mchog hor gong can/ 'jam dpal 'grel chen gyi dbang bka' dang bshad bka'/ 'jam dpal
gsang ldan gyi dbang bka' dang bshad bka' man ngag gi bka'/ 'jam dpal 'grel chung gi dbang dang bshad bka' man ngag gi bka'/ bram ze sdom bzang nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dpal
zab don du grags pa'i dbang bka' sogs dang / mar rngog gi lugs kyi gur brtag pa gsum man ngag dang bcas pa dang / dpyal lugs kyi gur brtag sam gsum/ 'gos kyi rdo rje gdan
gzhi'i dbang 'grel bcas/ gser sdings pas mdzad pa'i theg bsdus/ de'i khrid lta sgom spyod 'bras/ de dag gi rgyab rten du gyur pa'i mdo dang / rgyud rgya gzhung phal che
ba zhus/ gzhan yang gye re lha khang pa nas brgyud pa'i gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs

kyi dbang bka' sogs dang / pu hrang lo chung nas brgyud pa'i bde mchog lo hi pa'i dbang rgyud/ gnyos lugs kyi bde mchog lo hi pa'i dbang rgyud/ 'gos bsod nams rtse mo'i bde
mchog gi dbang rgyud/ steng pa lo tsA nas brgyud pa'i sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud/ rngog lugs kyi sgyu ma chen mo'i dbang bka' bshad bka' man ngag dang bcas pa/ do
ha skor gsum stod lugs smad lugs man ngag dang bcas pa/ bhu lu ka nas brgyud pa'i rlung 'chi med phyag len dang bcas pa/ mal lo nas brgyud pa'i sgrol ma nyer gcig gi dbang
sgrub skor dang bcas pa dang / 'khor lo chen po'i dbang chos skor/ chos rje sa skya paN chen gyis bsgyur ba'i yo ga'i rgyud gsum/ dze tA ri nas brgyud pa'i mi 'khrugs
pa'i dbang bka' sgrub skor dang bcas pa/ sa lugs kyi rnam rgyal lha dgu ma/ pu gcer lugs kyi rnam rgyal lha lnga bcu nga gsum ma rtog pa sgrub skor dang bcas pa/ mkhan po
bo dhi sa twa nas brgyud pa'i gtsug tor dri med kyi mchod chog chos skor dang bcas pa/ rgyal po mdo lnga/ zab mo mdo lnga la sogs pa'i mdo dang / byams chos lnga dang /
dbu ma rigs tshogs bstod tshogs/ springs yig gi tshogs dang tshig 'jug la sogs pa gsan no/ /de ltar kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer gyis bla ma 'di la chos kyi gtad sor dgongs
nas phyogs ris nas chos zhu ba byung ba rnams kyi gral bcug ste zab chos mang du gnang ngo / /de nas bla ma chos sku ba'i gsung gis/ da yon tan gzhan rnams thams cad phun
tshogs pa byung 'dug pas/ de thams cad kyi

mtshang 'dru zhing gdar sha chod pa la rigs pa dgos pas tshad ma rnam nges cis kyang slobs gsungs nas/ slob dpon chos dar la gtad nas rnam nges la slob gnyer mdzad pas gzhung
rdzogs par zin chos skad chags tsam byung ba dgung lo nyer lnga lon pa'i tshe bla ma chos sku ba zhi bar gshegs so/ /dgung lo nyer lnga'i mjug tu snar thang la byon nas/
der mkhan po skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ las slob dbu tshad pa rin chen bzang po/ gsang ston 'dul 'dzin sangs rgyas rgyal po rnams la zhus nas bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/
phyis su gsang ston la 'dul ba mdo rtsa tshar gsum gsan zhing / 'dul ba'i yan lag lag len dang bcas pa slob par mdzad/ de dag gi bar skabs bar skabs su bsam gling pa'i
bla ma dar ma rgyal mtshan dang / shes rab dpal ba la phag mo khros nag bka' gter gnyis/ mai tri pa'i bcu gsum ma'i dbang / zhi byed thugs rgyud/ phyag chen brda/ lam 'bras
bu dang bcas pa zha lugs la sogs pa gsan no/ /de nas bsam gling pa dang rtsa ba'i yon mchod yin pas/ pha gzhis thams cad bsam gling pa la phul nas/ dpal gro stag tshang
seng ge rdzong du byon/ de nas gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od kyi bu chen bla ma rdzong pa zhes bya ba nyams rtogs khyad par can mnga' ba zhig yod pa de'i spyan sngar/ sngar
bla ma chos sku ba'i drung du bka' thob byas pa'i lta sgom spyod 'bras kyi khrid/ lta ba dbu ma chen po a ti sha nas/ ser grog sngon pa nas brgyud pa'i

khrid rgyas pa/ dbu ma snying po'i khrid bsdus pa/ nyams len bsgom pa'i khrid la shes rab gtso bor byas pa phyag rgya chen po'i skor la/ phyag rgya chen po lhan cig skyes sbyor
rkyen bzhi go cha gnyis dang bcas pa/ phyag rgya chen po go cha lam khyer/ phyag rgya chen po rnal 'byor bzhi ldan/ rnal 'byor bzhi ldan gyi khrid rgyas pa/ rnal 'byor
bzhi ldan chung ba/ rnal 'byor bzhi ldan tshigs bcad ma rnams a ti sha nas dwags po ba la brgyud pa/ nA ro pa nas brgyud pa'i phyag rgya chen po thog babs/ phyag chen
snyan brgyud/ phyag chen gol shor bcad pa/ log phug pa'i rnal 'byor bzhi ldan/ phyag chen zab mo nying khu/ phyag chen rnal 'byor snying po/ mai tri pa nas brgyud pa'i phyag
chen bsam gtan thun 'jog phyag chen yid la mi byed pa rnams dang / thabs gtso bor byas pa la/ nA ro'i chos drug khrid skor cha lag dang bcas pa/ ma rgyud yang snying
zhes pa rim lnga dang chos drug bsres pa'i khrid/ rim lnga gdan rdzogs kyi man ngag rim lnga gdan thog gcig tu bsgom pa'i chung ngu / phag mo bsgom drug gi man ngag rgya
chen spyod pa la lam rim/ smon pa sems bskyed/ 'jug pa sems bskyed/ don dam sems bskyed/ rgyu 'bras bdun gyi lam/ theg chen blo sbyong dang / 'bras su rdzogs pa chen po'i
rgyal thabs spyi blugs kyi dbang / snyan brgyud kyi 'phrang / gsal ba gsang skor brgyud pa sde bzhi'i skor rnams zhus nas nyams khrid du bskyangs/ gdar sha bcad nas bla
ma'i drung du ku re zhus pa/

e ma gser sdings chos brgyud 'di/ /gras thag yun ring bcad gyur pas/ /bla ma snying la zhugs so snyam/ /sgro 'dogs sems la chod nas thal/ /de 'dra go ba'i 'phags pa lags/ /med
kyang ku re byas pa lags/ /skal ldan 'gro la phan gyur cig /ces gsungs so/ /de rnams kyi dbang byin rlabs thams cad dang / chos skyong kha che mgon nag dang / mgon nag
zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i skor dang bcas pa rnams bla ma chos sku pa'i drung du thob cing / der yang sgro 'dogs bcad pa las nam langs pa la nyi ma shar ba bzhin gyur te/
e ma ho/ kun mkhyen bla chen byin rlabs kyis/ /nam langs pa la nyi shar ltar/ /khyad par 'phags pa'i 'od ldan pa/ /deng sang kho bo yin pa snyam/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de nas
re zhig na lho sgor hor dmag zhugs nas zos mi bde dang / mu ge chen po byung nas 'tsho ba shin tu dka' bar byung ba'i tshe/ bud med gcig zan gyi gzugs brnyan mang po la
mar dang / 'khur ba la sogs pa mang pos brgyan nas lha la mchod pa byed kyin 'dug pas/ bla ma 'dis dgongs pa la mos 'di dag dor song ba dang blangs pas zhag 'ga' zhig gi
