thug thal 'ong ba 'dug snyam pa dang / mos mchod pa zin nas snod du bcug ste khur song ba na/ thugs la re ches na bslu dogs nas 'ching bar thag chod/ 'jig rten la re ba
bcad nas bcud len sna tshogs mdzad de lce chung gi bdud rtsi myang ba ka mchog tu byung gsungs/ de nas bod

du byon te mdzo pho lhas pa'i bla ma sangs rgyas bsgom pa zhes bya ba la sgang lo tsA ba'i lugs kyi rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang / 'phreng ba skor gsum bod kyi yig cha rgyas pa
dang bcas pa/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i rgyud/ gzhan yang bde mchog gi rgyud dang chos skor mang dag zhus/ khong la lam 'bras mi gcig pa bcu gcig gi bka' yod pa las bla ma
'dis bdun thob gsungs so/ /de nas bla ma chos sku ba'i gdan sa la dge bshes 'od zer mgon po bskos nas 'di'i mgo 'don khyed kyis gyis shig gsungs pa la brten nas khong la
slob gnyer byed pa dang / dbang bka' lung bka' sogs 'bogs pa/ bshad nyan gyi mgo 'don la sogs pa lo 'ga' mdzad dgos byung / de dag gi bar seng la drang so lung du mkhan
chen ka bzhi pa dkon gzhon la lam rim/ lam sgron/ be bum sngon po sogs dang / don yod zhags pa dang / phag mo'i skor rnams zhus/ ka bzhi pa thugs she la yang mngon pa kun
las btus kyi bshad pa tshar 'ga' zung mnyan zhing mngon pa'i gzhung phran mang po'i lung yang zhus/ de'i tshe sngar gyi dpon dge 'dun na re/ mkhan chen ka bzhi pa 'gran
gyi do med yin/ gzhan yang mkhas btsan bzang gsum gyi dge bshes brgya 'tshogs stong 'tshogs kyang / nga ni nga rang gi slob ma 'di ka la mos zer nas dbang dang khrid zhus
nyams myong yang bzang po byung nas cher dad par gyur to/ /de nas bla ma chos sku 'od zer gyi bu chen sre'u chung gi lce blo ldan seng ge'i drung du gsang 'dus rngog

lugs 'grel pa dang bcas pa dang / rgyud rkyang man ngag dang bcas pa/ gsang 'dus kyi bshad rgyud bzhi/ gnyos lugs kyi lo hi pa'i dbang bka'/ rtsa rgyud kyi bshad bka'/ bde
mchog gi bshad rgyud/ mngon brjod bla ma sogs/ rngog lugs kyi gur brtag sam gsum sgrub sde lnga bsre 'pho dbang bka' dang bcas pa/ rdo rje gdan bzhi'i dbang bka'/ rtsa rgyud
bshad rgyud sogs kyi bshad bka'/ ba lang rmig sogs kyi khrid bka' sgrub skor la dang bcas pa/ phyag rgya chen po gzhung gi skor la grub pa sde bdun/ snying po skor drug
aM nas nyer lnga/ bka' bskul gyi chos bzhi dang bcas pa/ yo ga rdo rje 'byung ba smad lugs kyi Tikka mi gcig pa tshar mang du gsan no/ /rdo rje rtse mo smad lugs/ dpal
mchog sher dum/ de'i nag 'byams shrardha'i thig rtsa rtsa 'grel/ kun snying dang pradznyA wa li tas mdzad pa'i spyan dbye cho ga rab 'byor skyong gi sbyin sreg gtsug dgu
smad lugs kyi dbang bka' bshad bka'/ kun rig smad lugs/ 'khyin lugs/ sgyur lugs gsum gyi dbang bka' bshad bka'/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang bka'/ gzungs sgrub skor dang bcas pa/
chab gtor 'jam dpal ma/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar/ tshe dpag med steng phyogs ma/ grub pa'i rgyal mo'i tshe sgrub/ rta mgrin nag po'i rjes gnang la sogs pa ched du gtad pa
dang / gzhan gyi zhor la byung ba'i chos sgo dpag tu med pa gsan no/ /de nas skabs shig tu bya btang du sku mtshams la bzhugs yod pa'i

tshe/ chos rje kun spangs pas 'dir rgyud 'grel zhig 'bri ba dang / dus 'khor gyi thang ka zhig 'bri ba yin pas 'dir 'khor tsam zhig shog gsungs pa bzhin byon pas/ rgyud rnying
zhig gsungs pa'i dbu tshugs nas 'dug pa dang / sngon la rgyud rnying 'di nyon cig gsungs pa la/ sngar bla ma chos sku ba'i drung du bzhugs dus zhal tsha ba zhig 'dug
pa nas chos ma zhus pa yin na'ang / da lam ma zhus par nyon gsungs pa 'di thugs la yod pa yin snyam nas mnyan pas/ rgyud rnying cung zad ma tshar ba la/ khyed yi ge 'bri
ba rkyang pa la bos pa min pas/ da res khrid 'di yang nyon gsungs nas sbyor drug gi khrid gnang ste lo gsum la yongs su rdzogs pa mdzad do/ /phyis bla ma'i gsung gis/ khyod
rang 'dod cing mi bde ba byung na zhu ba su 'dug pa'i zla la 'ong bas chog go gsungs nas/ phyis su snga phyir bsdoms pa'i khrid bdun zhus nas phyag len thams cad legs
par sbyangs/ gsung bgros thams cad zin bris mdzad/ srung 'khor dgos pa rnams dpe chung du bris te legs par gtan la phab nas/ 'bro lugs kyi sbyor drug gi man ngag yu mo'i
yig cha dang bcas pa thams cad dang / sha ba rI nas brgyud pa'i gzhung chung shog ril bzhi dang bcas pa dang / rtsa mi lugs kyi sbyor drug sde skor dang bcas pa/ sga los
mdzad pa'i yor drug gi skor phran tshegs dang bcas pa dang / sa lugs kyi pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyor drug ma rgyud kye rdo rje'i sbyor drug zhang tshal pa'i sbyor
drug sde skor dang dang bcas pa/ 'bro lo tsA ba'i sbyor drug

sreg pa lung pa'i sbyor drug gyi jo lugs kyi sbyor drug dpe med mchog gi sbyor drug paN chen shAkya shrI'i sbyor drug rwa pa'i sbyor drug rtswa mi'i sbyor 'phreng / a rgyan
pa'i snyan brgyud/ dbang mdor bstan la sogs pa'i rgyud phran/ gzhung phran/ mtshan brjod rtsa 'grel/ dus 'khor gyi dbang bka' la sogs mang du zhus so/ /de nas lam 'bras
kyi yig cha brtsams pa'i yig mkhan yang mdzad nas lam 'bras kyi skor thams cad rdzogs par zhus/ gzhan yang phyag chen gang gA ma dang / thugs rje chen po'i smar khrid/ nyi
zla bsgrub pa/ ye shes spyan sgrub la sogs pa'i man ngag rnams dang / dgongs 'dus la sogs pa rnying ma 'ga' yar dang / rdzogs chen sems phyogs dang / rgya'i ha shang gi
man ngag gi skor rnams gnang ngo / /de'i dus su bdag dus 'khor 'di la da dung slob gnyer zhig byed/ sgra tshad pa mkhas par grags gda' bas de'i drung du 'gro zhus pas/ de
tsho shes rab che bas shes rab kyi rtsal gyi bshad pa yin/ brgyud pa'i man ngag dang mi ldan pas der 'gro ba 'os min/ rwa 'bro gnyis ka'i brgyud pa'i man ngag gi gtugs
sa yin pas rong du song gsungs nas/ bla ma shes rab seng ge ba'i drung du byon/ dus kyi 'khor lo sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs kyi dbang zhus nas/ rgyud 'grel la sbyangs pa
mdzad nas/ dka' gnas la bshad pa zab pa byung tsam na 'phral du glegs shing la yi ger bris/ de'i 'phro rnams chos thun grol ba na zhus/ de yang yi ge la btab/

de nas chos thog phyi ma la de rnams mthun mi mthun bltas/ zin thun bris/ dpe chung dgos pa thams cad zhib par bkod/ phyag len dang bkag 'gog thams cad/ tha na rdor dril 'jog
lugs dang / phreng ba 'khyer lugs tshun chad la dri gtugs zhib par mdzad pas/ bla ma'i gsung gis/ khyed 'phags rgod yag ma bya ba rtsa ba lum bu bzhin ma bcad par ye mi
nyan pa'i mi yin pas dris shig gsungs nas lan legs par btab/ chos rdo rus thug pa zhig byed na dri ba de lta bu zhig dgos pa yin/ gzhan nga rang las mkhas pa dka'/ nga'i
rtsar yong gin yod pa yin nam/ dri ba de lta bu byed pa ye rang ma byung gsungs shing thugs mnyes tshor chen po mdzad/ de nas shambha lar/ khro dgon/ sha ra dgon/ gnam
rtse ldeng / gnas mo che la sogs gang bzhud par phyag phyir 'brangs nas/ rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa zhu thug mdzad/ de nas khrid zhus nas phyag bzhes kyi srol ji lta
ba bzhin bsgoms pas nyams rtogs la'ang bogs thon pa byung gsungs/ der dbang mdor bstan sogs dus 'khor gyi gzhung phran 'grel pa skor gsum/ na ro 'grel chen de'i man ngag
sgrom lde rtsa 'grel/ rwa lugs kyi sbyor drug bla ma shes rab seng ge bas mdzad pa'i sbyor drug gi yig cha/ 'bro lugs pa'i khrid skor/ yu mo'i yig cha mdud 'grol dang
bcas pa/ ston thun/ man lung pa'i sbyor drug sha ba ri'i sbyor drug man ngag snye ma/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa/ rwa lugs kyi nag 'jigs skor gsum/ sngon 'byung rnam gsum/ lha
mo rnam gsum/ mi g.yo ba rnal 'byor chen po bla med/ gzungs grwa lnga/ 'od zer can/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho la sogs pa mang du gsan zhing / phyis dus 'khor gyi bka' 'phrang
la yig cha

mdzad pa'i yig mkhan yang mdzad do/ /de nas chos rje kun spangs pa gshegs pa'i rjes su jo mo nang du byon pas/ byang sems rgyal ye'i dbon po rnams sbrad nas/ btsun chung 'di
pa slob gnyer byed du 'jug pa yin pas dus 'khor gsung ba zhu gsungs nas/ dpon pos gtso mdzad dge bshes mang po la dus 'khor 'grel chen rgyud rnying la sogs pa mang du gsungs
shing / de'i tshe bla ma byang sems rgyal ye la dus 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi dbang / rgyu rnying / grub rnying gi skor/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa sogs mang du zhus so/ /de
nas dbon pos bde chen du gdan drangs nas der yang gsungs shing / dus 'khor mkhas rab shes pa dang / blo kha phyogs pa dang dad pa thob pa mang du byung / der bla ma grags
chen pa dang zhal mjal nas chos phar zhu tshur zhu mang du mdzad de/ jo bo lugs kyi gsang 'dus 'phags skor gzhung phran man ngag dbang bka' khrid bka' dang bcas pa/ chag
lugs kyi gsang 'dus 'phags skor gzhung bshad dbang bka' gzhung phran dang bcas pa/ dpyal lugs kyi 'phags skor/ sa lugs kyi 'phags skor/ sa lugs kyi kyai rdor dang / bdag
med ma'i dbang byin rlabs sgrub skor dang / rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa/ gur mgon gyi skor la sgrub thabs las tshogs mang po dang bcas pa/ sa lugs kyi lU nag dril
gsum gzhung gdams ngag dang / jo bo lugs kyi lU nag dang / rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi dbang bka' bshad bka' man ngag dang bcas pa/ jo bo lugs

kyi kye rdor kyi dbang bka' rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' dang bcas pa/ jo bo lugs kyi mahA mA ya'i dbang bshad khrid dang bcas pa/ o rgyan sgrol ma'i dbang bka' chos skor dang
bcas pa/ stod lugs kyi rtse mo rigs bsdus dang gtsug dgu dbang sgrub thabs/ mi 'khrugs pa rnal 'byor rgyud du byas pa'i jo bo lugs/ bya rgyud du byas pa'i sa lugs/ rnam
'joms bir lugs dang / ba ri lugs/ don zhags sa lugs kyi rjes gnang chos skor dang bcas pa/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs gdon grol chung ngu dang bcas pa/ ri khrod lo ma can
gsar rnying / dpal mo'i bcu gcig zhal gyi sgrub thabs snyung gnas dang bcas pa/ jo bo'i yi ge drug pa gtso 'khor gsum pa dang / thugs rje chen po skyer sgang lugs gnyis
kyi rjes gnang chos skor dang bcas pa/ jo bo'i mi g.yo ba spyan gnyis/ gser gling pa'i mi g.yo ba dmigs pa skor gsum blo bdeg dang bcas pa/ sa lugs kyi mi g.yo ba nag po
las tshogs dang bcas pa/ sa lugs kyi gza' yum mchod chog dang bcas pa/ phyag brgyad sgrol ma/ gnas brtan bcu drug gi gsol 'debs/ chab gtor dang char 'bebs la sogs pa mang
duzhus gsungs/ de'i tshe la stod nas bla ma grags pa dpal zhes bya ba drung du chos zhu ru byung ba la u rgyan pa'i bsnyen sgrub kyi skor rnams zhus so/ /rin po che tshogs
dang gnyags kyi slob ma bla ma bsod nams mgon zhes bya ba la/ sa lugs kyi bde kye yo ga gsum/ rnam rgyal 'joms/ gdon sgrol

gtor chen rnams rnying ma lugs kyi lag len zhib par bslabs so/ /de nas bo dong er byon snur chor 'phags rgyal mtshan la yo ga stod lugs pa'i 'grel pa la brten pa'i dbang bka'/
de nyid 'dus pa'i rgyud/ stod 'grel smad 'grel/ rdor 'byung sems dpa' 'byung chung / ko sa la'i rgyan a wa ta ra/ dpal mchog smad 'grel/ phyag na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
la 'jig rten pa drug btags pa'i sbyong rgyud kyi dbang bka'/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi rtogs pa gnyis/ tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra/ kha 'bar ma'i gzungs gnyis/ tshul
brgya lnga bcu pa la sogs pa gsan no/ /khong pas kyang lta sgom spyod 'bras la sogs pa mang du zhus so/ /de'i tshe bla ma byang sems rgyal ye'i dbon po 'ongs nas bu chen
thams cad kyi dgon pa bde chen 'dzin par zhus pas/ dgon chung sdug bsngal gyi btson rar dgongs nas mdzad du ma bzhes par/ dbon chung la slob gnyer mdzub khrid du mdzad
nas bskos so/ /de nas stod phyogs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen khrid zhu/ dbang zhu/ lung zhu zer ba mang po byung nas/ nyin rang lung dang bshad pa mdzad/ mtshan rang cho ga
mdzad de nyin mtshan khor yug chos 'chad pa la 'bad pa mdzad kyang / 'jig rten blos btang nas sgrub pa mthar 'don pa cher ma byung / po ti rkang btsugs nas slob gter byed
pa'ang mang po ma byung bas thugs 'jungs te/ chos kyi rnam grangs gsog pa'i lung thob tshod ma tshwa blta ba lta bu 'di la dgos pa mi 'dug dgongs nas/

nyang stod skyid mkhar lha khud kyi phu ru spe chung gcig pu zhig tu sku mtshams bcad nas sgrub pa snying por mdzad kyin bzhugs so/ /de lta bu'i bla ma 'phags 'od yon tan rgya
mtshos/ bu ston rin po che thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub la gsang ba 'dus pa 'gos rdog lugs/ mar lugs/ jo bo lugs/ chag lugs sogs thams cad gnang ba yin no/ /de yang
bla ma 'phags 'od nyang stod du sgrub pa la bzhugs pa'i tshe bu ston rin po ches gsang 'dus skor gsan par bzhed nas/ dge bshes bsod nams rin chen bya ba rin po che'i
me tog dang bcas/ bdag gsang ba 'dus pa zhig don du gnyer ba lags pas thugs la btags dgos/ de la bdag der drung du 'ongs na mchi'am/ bla ma khyed 'dir byon pa gang gi legs
kyi skabs dbyer gsol zhes pa'i zhu ba 'phags 'od kyi drung du btang bas/ thog mar mjal kha ma gnang nas/ zhu yig dang gser gyi me tog phul bas gzod mjal kha byung ste/
bla ma 'phags pa'i zhal nas khyed nor ba min nam/ nga ni btsun rgan gcig kyang mi shes pa ma Ni bgrangs nas sdod pa zhig yin/ khong la dgos pa'i gsang 'dus de 'dra ngas mi
shes/ nga la snying thag mda' rgyang las ring ba la sogs pa yod pa'i yon tan dang kha na so med pa la sogs med pa'i yon tan mang po yod te/ de tsho ni khong la mi mkho
mchi/ khyed rang gser khur la log rgyugs gsungs pa na/ khong gis nor ba min pa 'dug dus 'khor slob pa'i dus su bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan pas khyed la gsang

'dus mkhas po yod byas nas khungs bstan par 'dug dge slong shAkya dpal gyis kyang ngo shes kyis 'dug ma nor byas pas/ slob dpon rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mgo skor byas 'dug
pa/ ngas dang po gsang 'dus shig nyan myong ste brjed nas med pas/ ngas khong pa'i slob dpon gang nas 'ong / cis kyang gsang 'dus don du gnyer na/ sre'u chung ba dang khong
pa'i slob ma bsod she dang / sangs rgyas dpal la sogs mang po yod pas der zhus gsungs/ de tsho la zhu 'dod mi gda'/ cis kyang drung du zhu bar gda' zhus pas/ der 'phags
'od kyi zhal nas dge bshes gsan dang / phyi dus kyi byed pa yol/ dus snyigs pas chos zhu ba thams cad kyang bka' thob tsam lung thob las rtsa ba gcod mkhan yong ba mi
'dug chos bshad mkhan rnams kyang spyang a pho'i klog bri pa ji bzhin las rdo rus gtugs la bshad rgyu yod pa mi 'dug sgos su nang dus kyi byed pa yol/ legs par rgas/ dran
pa mi gsal/ bshad 'phro la brjed kyi 'gro/ rna ba rtse chag mig mi gsal/ 'di bzhin song ba yin mod gsungs nas nas dbu dang phyag la sogs pa bstan nas/ ngas khong pa'i slob
dpon mi 'ong gis log la song gsungs te log byung ba na/ khong yong ba'i nub mo bu ston rin po che'i mnal lam du mthongs khung lta bu zhig gi pha rol na rdor dril gcig
dang / bum pa zhig 'dug pa/ len 'dod nas mi zhig la de pa tshur thongs gsungs pas/ mi des myur du gtong ma 'dod pa la/ nga rang rgyang gis mchongs la blang dgos dgongs pa
na

mnal sad/ de nas nangs par de khong sleb byung nas/ bla ma khong ni chos ye gsungs ba'i rigs su mi 'dug de bas gzhan la zhus na rang 'thad dam zhu ba la/ bu ston gyi zhal nas/
khong thugs la btags/ nga cis kyang yong ga la gsungs/ spos 'dod pa la mi ro bam pos ci bya/ khyed rang da dung phar song la der kho bo cis kyang yong bar 'dug pas dus
ci tsam la yong ba 'thad ces zhus shig bsgos te gnang / des kyang ji skad gsungs bzhin 'phags 'od kyi drung du phyin te zhus pas/ 'o na thag chod kyi mi la bshol 'debs
dka' bas khas blangs pa la thug go /khong la khyed kyis 'dir 'ongs kyang khang chung gcig pu las med pas nged der 'ong pa yin mod kyang / da lam dpe cha rnams kyang la stod
du lus 'dug pas/ de dag kyang blangs la chos 'khor thon pa dang cis kyang yong gsungs shig gsungs/ de lta bu'i lon nangs par yong ba'i do nub de/ bu ston rin po che'i
mnal lam du sngar mnal lam du byung pa'i bum pa de la kha rgyan dang mgul chings kyi rgyan dang bcas chu yis cung zad ma khengs pa zhig bud med cig gis khyer byung nas/ 'di
rtsa ba khyod rang gi yin te/ na ning nas brag ri na yar la 'khyar ba yin/ da khyod rang la gtad pa yin no zer nas gtad pa gsal po zhig rmi/ gzhan yang btsun pa 'dra ba
yang / rnal 'byor pa 'dra ba zhig gis sngar nas mnal lam du byung ba'i rdor dril de gtad pa snyam byed pa byung / de'i nangs par 'phags 'od kyi bka' gnang ba de 'byor/
de nas phyis chos 'khor thon nas bla ma 'phags 'od

yon tan rgya mtsho sku na bgres por song ba des/ bu ston rin po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar zha lur byon nas/ bu ston rin po che la khyed la rgya ba'i rgya lugs dang gar ba'i gar
lugs nas dgos pa'i lugs min/ bshar te bklags la skabs skabs su 'gag re tsam bshad de chos thob che bar byed pa yin no gsungs pa la/ bu ston rin po ches/ de 'dra'i lung
thob tsam gyis mi phan/ bshad pa rdo rus thug pa lag len dang bcas pa zhu 'tshal zhus pas/ 'phags 'od kyi zhal nas/ 'a pa yes snying nas rang gsang 'dus shes pa cig bzhed
dam gsungs/ shin tu 'dod lags zhus pas/ 'o na gsang 'dus kyi don rim lngar 'dus pa yin/ rim lnga'i khrid bzang po zhig thob na gsang 'dus kyi don rang rdol la yong bas
thog mar dbang dang khrid byed dgos gsungs nas dbang bka' bdun po gcig tu 'dus pa'i dbang bka' rgyas pa mdzad nas de nas 'dus pa'i rim lnga smar khrid dgun stod la rdzogs
par mdzad de/ slar dpyid ka rdog lugs/ mar lugs/ jo bo lugs/ chag lugs rnams kyi bshad bka'/ lung bka'/ man ngag gi bka' thams cad legs par stsal ba yin no/ /de ltar bu
ston rin po ches 'phags 'od la legs par gsan nas bstan pa'i khur chen po bzhes te/ 'dus pa la yig cha yang / sgron gsal gyi rnam bshad mtha' drug rab gsal/ 'dus pa'i sgrub
thabs dngos grub char 'bebs/ bstod pa byin rlabs char 'bebs/ gtor chog 'dod don char 'bebs/ dkyil chog ye shes char 'bebs/

sbyin sreg 'phrin las char 'bebs/ rgyud kyi bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ rim lnga'i khrid yig yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin chen za ma tog la sogs pa yig 'jogs rgya chen po
mdzad/ 'chad nyan rtsal du ston nas mdzad pas 'dus pa'i bdag po lta bur gyur pa yin la/ de dag gi nang nas khrid yig 'di ni kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer gyis 'phags 'od la
mar 'gos gnyis char gyi gdams pa gnang ba'i gsung bgros yi ger bris pa nyung ngu zhig yod pa de tshang bar bcug cing de'i steng du 'phags 'od kyi gsung bgros rnams bris
pa yin par bshad cing / ngo bo dben gsum yan 'gos lugs dang / sgyu ma dang 'od gsal mar lugs gtso bor byas pa zhig yin pa dang / sgyu ma'i skabs su mnyam bzhag sgyu ma la
sbyor drug gi dmigs pa gcig kyang bcug yod pas/ de yang kun mkhyen chos sku ba sbyor drug pa yin pas/ khong gis bsnan pa bzhin bu ston gyis kyang 'bri bar mdzad pa yin
par grags so/ /gzhan yang sgyu ma gsum btud du bya ba sogs nag khrid bsres pa dang / zung 'jug gi skabs su bsdus se ba zhig gi mar lugs 'gos lugs gnyis ka dang mthun pa zhig
yod par mkhas pa snga ma rnams bzhed mod kyang / khrid yig de nyid kyi dbang bskur/ rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i don bshad pa'i rgyud bzhi'am brgyad kyi
dgongs pa legs par phye shing / 'phags pa klu sgrub yab sras kyi don mngon du gyur nas dgongs pa legs par bkral te tai lo pa dang nA ro pa la sogs pa

mkhas grub rnams kyi thugs dam du legs par bstar nas zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa'i man ngag rgyud sde zab mo thams cad kyi sgo 'byed pa'i lde mig lam rim pa lnga'i smar khrid
ces sogs gsungs pas na/ bu ston rin po che'i lugs kyi gsang ba 'dus pa'i khrid 'di mar lugs gtso che ba dang / rgyud 'grel ba dang bcas pa'i bshad bka' 'gos nas rdog pa
la brgyud pa'i lugs gtso che bar rang lugs kyi phyis byon pa'i mkhas pa dag bzhed/ dbang bka' ni bka' babs so so'i lugs kun 'dus pa zhig ste/ de nas bzung ste gsang ba
'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang gi brgyud pa la brgyud pa'i bka' babs bdun ldan zhes dbang zhig thob pa na brgyud pa bka' babs bdun char gyi brgyud pa drangs chog pa 'di byung
bas/ bsres brgyud ces pa'i tha snyad btags su rung ngam snyam mo/ /yang 'ga' zhig las klu byang gi dkyil chog nyi shu pa'i rjes 'brangs kyi dkyil chog la 'phags pa rin
po che'i dkyil chog dang / bu ston gyi dkyil chog ye shes char 'bebs gnyis 'dren pa yang mdzad 'dug pa ltar/ rje btsun sa paN gyis kha che paN chen la gsan pa'i dbang bka'
gsar ma'i khongs su bsdu dgos pa yang 'dra bas brtag go /de rnams kyis 'gos lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas 'gos lugs ji ltar dar ba'i tshul bstan
zin pa yin la/ bu ston man chad kyi brgyud rim rnams ni 'og tu mar lugs dang / sa lugs kyi brgyud pa dag dang phal cher chab gcig tu 'byung ngo / /gnyis pa mar lugs
kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i

rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas lugs de nyid ji ltar dar ba'i tshul ni/ skyes mchog mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyis blo gros kyi legs par spel ba la gsang 'dus mar lugs su grags pa
yin te/ de nyid lo tsA ba nas rim gyis brgyud/ mkhas pa phyi ma dag gis 'phel rgyas su mdzad pas deng sang gi bar du yang dar rgyas su bzhugs pa yin te/ de yang mar pa lo
tsA ba 'di lho brag dbus dpe gsar bya bar yab mar pa mon pa'am mar pa dkon mchog bya ba'i sras su sku 'khrungs/ las 'phro mang mkhar mu gu lung du sad de/ thugs rgya gar
'phags yul du sbyangs/ 'bras bu bod kha ba can du smin te/ de yang mar pa 'di dang po gzhon nu dus su thugs shin tu gtum pa mi phal cher mi smon pa zhig yin pa las/ dgung
lo bcu gsum pa la chos sgor zhugs/ yab kyi pha spun yin pa'i chos pa zhig yod pa de'i drung du slob gnyer la btang bas/ chos ma bslab par sdang gtser byed pa zhig byung
pas/ gser mang po bskur nas lo tsA slob par gzhan du btang bas/ mar pas rim gyis dbus kyi lho brag nas gdan bteg ste/ de dus kha ba can na'ang 'brog mi lo tsA ba mkhas
pa dang man ngag gi snyan pa che bas/ thog mar mu gu lung na 'brog mi bzhugs pa'i drung du byon nas lo tsA legs par bslabs/ chos gzhan 'ga' re yang zhus/ lo gcig gi bar du
mu gu lung du bzhugs nas gdams pa zhus kyang rgyud dang gdams pa zab mo ye ma gnang nas/ lho bal du 'gro dgos dgongs pa na/ de nyid bla mas dgongs nas/ 'brog bla chen gyi
zhal nas/ lo tsA ni mkhas par khyed rang gis shes/

da rgyud gdams ngag zhu ba la/ khyod kyis sngar gyi zhabs tog gis cung mi yong bas/ yang na yul du log la rgyags thub pa long la shog yang na khyed rang gis byin pa'i rta 'di
yang phar byin gyi/ gser du tshong la bal po tsam du chos zhu ba la dka' las ci 'dug tshod lta ba la song dang / gzod nga la yang gus pa drin du gzo ba zhig yong ste mchis
gsungs/ der bla ma mar pas sngar khong rang gis phul ba'i rta nag po seng ge kha gdangs zhes bya ba tshur zhus nas/ zab chen bub cig seng ldeng gi rta sga gcig dang
gsum rtag rigs su 'tshong du phyin pas gser srang nyi shu khugs nas/ dge bshes klokya chen pos grogs mdzad nas rim gyis bal por byon te/ lam gyi dka' ba dpag tu med pa byung
yang dang du bzhes pa yin te/ de nyid kyi gsung las/ nags 'thug po gcig la thon dus med/ /lam ring po gcig la bgrod dus med/ /gcan gzan 'phrang dang chu la thar dus med/
/lam de kun ni bde dog mthong tsam na/ /bya dgung la 'phur ba'ang gshog rtse 'dar/ /zhes gsungs/ de nas bal por bal po spyi ther ba la rdo rje gdan bzhi la sogs pa'i
chos mang du gsan kyang / des kyang thugs ma tshim pa lus srog khyad du bsad de/ rgya gar du gshegs te/ nyid kyi gsung las/ rgya gar gyi yul du phyin tsam na/ /mtha' 'khob
kyi jag pa shi skyid la/ /srog ci bder thon pa cung ma bsams/ /gcan gzan gyi ngar skad thos tsam na/ /lus gtsang mar thon pa yid la byed/ /sbrul sbram chen gyi kha rlangs

mthong tsam na/ /yid brtan por phyin kyang gom tshugs 'khyor/ /lam de kun gyi tsha grang bshad tsa na/ /dus da lta dran yang blo snying 'dar/ /zhes dang / chos snying nas 'tshol
ba'i gdung sems skyes/ /yul rgya gar shar nub chu bzhin nyul/ /thang chen po gcig la pha mtha' med/ /mya ngan gyi thang la phyin no snyam/ /yid chos la bsams kyang
snying rlung 'phyo/ /nad 'tsho bar dka' ba'i tshad pas thebs/ /lar de shi de chad bcu gsum byung / /kha chems kyang tshig gsum bzhag sa med/ /dbugs 'gyu ba chad pa lan gsum
myong / /dus de kun gyi bde sdug myong tsam na/ /sdang dgra yi mig nas mchi ma 'chor/ /zhes gsungs so/ /tshul de lta bu'i dka' spyad bzhed de rgya gar du phebs/ paNDi
ta su mkhas dris pas/ mai tri pa dang / nA ro pas grub pa thob zer bas/ thog mar mai tri pa la gser phul nas zhus pas/ ngas bla ma dang sprad kyis gsungs nas/ nA ro pa can
btang / mar pas byon pas zla ba drug tu ma mjal/ de'i dus su mar pa la sa gdon gyi snyun thu mo zhig byung nas/ nA ro pa'i rnag gsol bas snyun las grol/ de nas nA ro pa
sku khams bsang ba sogs kyi rjes su 'brengs te maNDal 'bul zhing gsol ba btab pas/ zla ba drug nas mjal kha gnang ste 'dus pa'i dbang dang / rim lnga smar khrid/ rgyud kyi
bshad pa hril tsam dang bcas pa stsal zhing lo drug dang zla ba bdun gyi bar mar pas nA ro pa'i drung du bzhugs/ de nas bod du byon la stod dger phu ru klo skya ston pas
sna len byas te/ chos 'chad cing lo gcig bzhugs/ de nas dbu ru byang ngos

su byon/ mar pa mgo legs bya bas sna len byas te chos bshad pas/ mgo legs kyis gser srang bcu gnyis phul/ de nas gser bre gang tsam byung ba khyer te/ rgya gar du bla ma dang
mjal bar byon pas/ nA ro pa spyod pa la gshegs nas mi bzhugs pas/ dgon par jo mo la tshogs 'khor gcig byas gsol ba btab pas zhal mjal gser phul nas chos zhus pas/ dges
rdor dang gdan bzhi bde mchog sogs gnang nas shes sam lan gsum gsungs/ shes lags zhus/ slar yang bde mchog gi chos cig zhu snyam tsa na gar gshegs cha ma byung yang maNDal
phul gsol ba btab pas/ ri zur zhig la bzhugs pa mthong nas der byon pas/ nA ro pa rnag ka pA li gang mi rtsibs kyis gsol nas grub pa na/ ka pA li kha phub song ba/ mar
pas blangs te lhag ma byogs nas gsol bas/ ro shin tu zhim pa zhig 'dug nas lhag ma lus pa gsol/ ka pA li bsnams te sras la gtad/ de ltar bla ma mar pa 'dis spyir 'phags
yul du lan gsum/ bal por lan gsum ste rgya bal du chos kyi ched kho nar lan drug byon te/ rgya gar shar nub lho byang kha che bal po sogs thams cad nyul/ paNDi ta dang ku
sa lir grags pa bla ma brgya rtsa brgyad/ bshad srol 'dzin pa lnga bcu/ snang ba 'gyur nges bcu gsum/ lhag par gsang ba 'dus pa gsan pa'i bla ma bdun/ khyad par du 'phags
pa'i bla ma bzhi sogs mkhas grub dpag tu med pa zhig bsten pa yin te/ nyid kyi gsung las/ zhabs pad spyi bor reg mdzad cing / /gsung don

bdud rtsi'i rjes gnang ba/ /chos 'brel tsam gyi bla ma mang / /dpal singga gling pas sna drangs pa/ /snang ba 'gyur nges bcu gsum bzhugs/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gzhan yang bal
po spyi ther ba/ ye shes snying po/ zhi ba bzang po/ mai tri pa/ nA ro paN chen sogs grub thob lnga yod de/ chos smon lam gyi 'brel pa bcu gsum bzhugs/ /khyad par grub
thob zhal snga bzhugs/ /zhes gsungs/ de rnams kyi nang nas ye shes snying po la nub gu la kShe tra zhes bya ba'i gnas su rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa dang / man ngag sgyu lus
dang 'od gsal/ 'dus pa rim lnga'i gdams ngag rnams zhus/ byang phu la ha ri bya bar nA ro pa la rgyud dges pa rdo rje dang / man ngag bsre 'pho gsan/ shar chu bo ganggAr
mai tri pa la rgyud bstod pa glur blangs dang / man ngag phyag rgya chen po gsan/ lho dug mtsho khol mar dpal zhi ba bzang po la rgyud ma hA mA ya dang / man ngag dbyibs
rnal 'byor gsum bya ba gsan pas 'di bzhi la khyad par du 'phags pa'i bla ma bzhi zhes kyang bya'o/ /de ltar yang nyid kyi gsung las/ nub gu la kShe tra'i grong khyer du/
/dpal ye shes snying po'i zhabs la gtugs/ /sgyu lus 'od gsal gyi gdams ngag thob/ /lam rim pa lnga yi don la bslabs/ /zhes sogs gsungs pas so/ /de bzhi'i nang nas kyang rgyal
sras mai tri pa dang paN chen nA ro pa gtso bo lta bur mdzad de/ ji skad du/ rje 'gran gyi do med rnam gnyis bzhugs/ /gtso bo pan chen nA ro pa/ /de 'og rgyal sras mai
tri pa/ /zhes gsungs/ de ltar

mkhas grub gnyis ldan gyi bla ma mang du bsten pas gsang 'dus rim lnga'i smar khrid mi the ba'i rdzogs rim zab mo'i khrid brgya rtsa brgyad bzhugs pa yin te/ rim lnga'i smar
khrid ma gtogs pa'i/ /rdzogs rim brgya dang brgya rtsa shes/ /che na ngo mtshar de che mod/ /ces gsungs so/ /de ltar rje mar pas/ rgya gar gyi yul du lan gsum phyin/ /nA
ro paN chen gyi byin gyis brlabs/ /bsgoms te sangs ni kun kyang rgya/ /ma bsgoms rgya na rgya ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar 'phags yul du lan gsum byon pa'i snga phyi kun
bsdoms pas lo bco brgyad bzhugs/ spyir chos mang du lobs/ khyad par gsang ba 'dus pa rgyud rkyang man ngag dang bcas pa dang / rim lnga'i smar khrid snying po'i don hril
gyis dril bsogs gsan te/ de nas brgyud pa la sgro 'dogs nang nas gcod pa grub thob nyams kyi brgyud pa zhes grags/ yang dpal ye shes snying po la 'dus pa'i rtsa rgyud bshad
rgyud 'grel ba 'grel bshad dang bcas pa sogs rgyas par zhus/ de nas brgyud pa la mkhas pa paNDi ta'i lugs sam brgyud pa zhes grags so/ /de lta bu'i skyes mchog mar pa
lo tsA chos kyi blo gros la slob ma'i mchog kyang / grong 'jug gi bka' babs rang gi rigs sras dar ma mdo sde/ 'pho ba'i bka' babs dol gyi tshur ston dbang gi rdo rje/ bshad
rgyud kyi bka' babs gzhung gi rngog chos sku rdo rje/ 'od gsal kyi bka' babs gtsang rong gi mes ston tshon po/ bde drod kyi bka' babs gung thang gi mid la ras pa sogs
byon pa'i phyi ma 'di bzhi la mnyes

pa'i bu bzhi'am/ ka chen bzhi zhes grags te/ snga ma gsum gyis bde kye sogs bshad pa'i srol bzung / mid las bka' babs bzhi'i gi gdams pa'i bcud sgrub pa'i srol bzung ba yin
no/ /gzhan yang chu gong dpal le/ dri ma'i bu chung / dol pa bdag ston/ dge bshes gad pa bzhi la bka' babs bu bzhi zhes dang / 'dam gyi mar mi mgo legs/ dger phu'i klog
skya jo sras/ 'phan yul nya ma dpal mo/ rkyang ro zhang ston bzhi la las can gyi slob ma bzhi zhes bya zhing / de rnams kyi nang nas tshur ston dbang gi rdo rje la 'dus pa'i
dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa gdams pa ni deng sang gi bar du dar rgyas su yod pa 'di nyid yin la/ de yang tshur ston 'di mthu la shin tu mnga' brnyes pa zhig yin
pas mthu'i sgo nas mi mang po bsad pa la 'gyod pa skyes nas/ mar pa la sdig po che btsan thabs su sangs rgya ba'i gdams pa yod zer ba thos te zhu ru phyin te/ de'i dus su
mar pas pha spun kha cig la dbang bskur ba'i phyag rgya mo mdzad pas/ nged kyi mi dma' phab zer nas bla ma mar pa'i grwa pa'i rta la mda' brgyab/ rta rdzi brdungs/ 'o dod
'bod du bcug pas/ bla ma mar pa thugs khros te zhal nas/ ngas rgya gar du sangs rgya ba'i gdams pa min pa/ bstan srung rang mi dgos snyam nas mthu sogs ma zhus pa yin
na'ang / da ngan pa 'di tsho'i sdig gsog du 'ong ba 'dug pas/ nga snub zam nag pa can du mthu zhu ru 'gro bas khyed rang tsho gyes shig gsungs pa la/ tshur ston gyis ku re
ma lags sam/ mthu dgos na bdag gis bgyi'am zhus pas/ 'o na gyis shig gsungs

nas/ nya la dus btab/ tshes gcig nas mthu bsgrubs pas/ der phas spun pos kyang sha chang mang po la mi mang po bsags nas/ mar pas 'o skol la mthu dus btab pas/ ma shi na lha
gsol/ shi na dge rtsa byed zer/ de nas tshes bcu'i bar du rtags gang yang ma byung nas/ bla ma'i zhal nas/ kho la ni cham pa'i nad tsam yang mi 'dug gyad kyi mthu sdug
sam gsungs pas/ tshur ston na re/ da rung mi shes zhag gcig ma thim zhus/ de nas nya'i nub mo gzer gyis btab nas shi ba na/ khrab dang rta mang po gnang bas/ tshur gyi bla
ma mar pa'i sku pang du mgo bo bzhag nas/ sdig po che bdag la gdams ngag med/ dmyal bar 'gro ba ya cha zhus nas bshums pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas/ ngu mi dgos yar la longs
dang gsungs/ khyod 'jigs mi dgos nga la sdig po che btsan thabs su sangs rgya ba'i gdams ngag yod kyi gsungs nas/ gsang ba 'dus pa rim lnga'i gdams pa zab mo rdzogs par gnang
/ khyad par btsan thabs su sangs rgya ba'i gdams pa zab mo gnang bas/ tshur mnyes te/ sgyu ma'i nor rdzas thun mong lags/ /bstan srung 'di la yon tan gda'/ /bla ma mnyes
pa'i yon tan gda'/ /bla ma mnyes pas gdams ngag gnang / /btsan thabs sangs rgyas bdag la gnang / /zhes gsungs nas bsgoms pas rtogs pa phul du phyin pa thugs rgyud la
'khrungs so/ /de lta bu'i tshur dbang gi rdo rjes/ 'khon gad pa kIrti la 'dus pa'i gdams ngag yongs su rdzogs pa gnang

ba yin te/ de yang dam pa 'di dang po shab na tshad ma la gsan sbyong mdzad nas bzhugs pa'i tshe/ gyi ston gyis/ mtshan nyid kyi chos kyis ci byed/ de nas myur du sangs rgya
ba'i gdams ngag dga' mod zer bas/ khong gis 'o na de 'dra'i gdams pa su la yod byas pas/ rnal 'byor 'dis tshur dbang gi rdo rje la yod zer bas/ mtshan thos pa tsam gyis
bun byed pa sogs mos gus 'khrungs nas/ rta rgod ma gcig yod pa la tshos tang bzhi bkal tshur can byon nas mjal kha zhus pas/ jo mo na re/ mtshams bcad pas mjal kha mi 'ong
zer yang / sngar gyi slob ma zhig yin cis kyang mjal dgos zhus te/ rta ra gcig tu khal phog nas bsdad pas/ srod la mjal kha gnang ste/ mar me 'od gsal ba las sngags pa
chen po gcig 'dug pa mthong nas/ zhal mthong ma thag sa gang yin/ nam mkha' gang yin cha med pa'i zi bun pa zhig byung / der bla ma'i zhal nas/ khyed nga'i slob ma min par
'dug gang nas yin gsungs/ lho phyogs pa zhig lags zhus/ de nas khong gi thugs la rta 'di bla ma la phul/ tshos kyis rgyags byas gdams pa zhu snyam pa la/ bla ma de la
mos gus che ba zhig skyes nas/ rta dang tshos thams cad phul bas/ gsang ba 'dus pa rim lnga'i gdams pa ma lus pa gnang / thugs nyams su bzhes pas sgyu ma'i rnam par skyes
te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams thams cad mthong ba dang / gzhan yang gang du bzhugs pa'i dus gcig so ba nag gi la rgyab na phar tshong ba su di ri ri 'gro ba thogs med
du gzigs pa la sogs pa mngon

par rtogs pa'i yon tan dpag tu med pa mnga' ba zhig yin no/ /de lta bu'i 'khon gad pa kIrtis/ byang khang pa bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa ma lus pa stsal ba yin te/ de yang
byang khang pa 'di 'khon gad pa kIrti dang yum gcig pa'i sku mched kyang yin zhing / gad pa ba la rim lnga'i gdams pa zhus pas/ 'khon gad pa la dges pa'i gsung gis/ slob
dpon pa byon pa legs/ chos bdag po la len du byon pa yin nam/ nga'i man ngag 'di rta zan bzhin bcang bcangs pa yin/ phag pa dbyar lam du tshud pa dang 'dra 'khyog sa med
pa zhig yin/ zan lhag gi lugs kyi mi che ba yin/ gdams ngag gi lugs kyi mi mang ba yin gsungs shing / man ngag rdzogs par dbu snyung bzhes nas man ngag yongs su rdzogs
par gnang ngo / /nyams rtogs kyi yon tan yang sgyu ma'i rnam thar 'khrungs pa sogs dpag tu med pa mnga' bas/ mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyi rnam
thar gyi cha shas dang tshul mtshungs par mdoms kyi mtshan ma rta cang shes ltar sbubs su nub pa dang / dbu'i gtsug tor gyen du 'phags pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba mang
du byung ba dang / zhi bar gshegs la khad kyi tshe nga'i pur 'di ma sbyang bar nub phyogs su kha ston la zhog gsungs/ thur lha'i mchod khang du de ltar byas nas bzhugs su
gsol bas/ de skabs rgya mkhar stod du srad pa'i rta jag gis yul mi chags pa lta bu'i zos ma bde yod pa rgyun chad pa'i lo rgyus kyang yod par grags so/ /de nyid kyis

thang spe mkhan po tshul khrims skyabs la 'dus pa'i man ngag rdzogs par gnang ba yin te/ thang spe ba 'di ni mdo sde dang rgyud sde thams cad la mkhyen pa thogs med du rgyas
pa/ lo bcu gnyis su sham thabs ma bzhes par stan thog gcig tu sgom sgrub mdzad pas rtogs pa chen po 'khrungs te/ bskyed pa'i rim pa la brtan pa thob/ rdzogs pa'i rim pa
la rtags thon/ ngag rdo rje'i bzlas par 'byongs/ snang ba sgyu lus su 'byongs/ thugs 'od gsal gyi ngang la bzhugs/ zung 'jug gi ting nge 'dzin la mnga' brnyes pas snang
ba la gnyis 'dzin gyi rtog pa zil gyis non pas/ dus rtag tu 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi bzhugs tshul dang mthun par bzhugs te 'gro don mdzad pa zhig yin par bshad do/ /des thang
spe ba 'phags pa skyabs la 'dus pa mar lugs yongs su rdzogs pa gnang ste/ 'di'i rnam thar ni gong du bstan zin la/ des grub thob gser sding pa gzhon nu 'od/ des kun
mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ des 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub la gnang ba yin no/ /yang khon gad pa kIrtis/ mi nyag thur ba la/
dbus pa mgar dga'/ grub thob zhang zhung pa chos kyi dbang phyug ste thugs sras gsum la gnang / de gsum char la/ gang bar gser kha'i rin chen gling pa tshul khrims mdzes
kyis zhus/ des rgya rnal 'byor pho ba lung pa la gdams te/ 'dis rim lnga bsdus gsal gyi 'grel pa sogs mar lugs kyi yig cha mang du mdzad/ des dge slong chos grags bzang
po/

bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/ bla ma blo ldan de nyid la yang 'phags 'od kyis gsan no/ /yang mar lugs kyi dbang bka' tsam gyi brgyud pa ni/ 'khon gad pa kIrtis/ yang lung zur dgon
pa mgar ston sher rgyal la gnang / des gnyen rtse aM phug pa sprul sku rin chen seng ge go lung pa ye shes rgyal/ rong ston mkhan po byang chub zung / gshong lo brtan/
lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge de la bu ston rin po ches gsan/ yang aM phug pa rin chen seng ge nas/ rong pa sher bzang / ston mo lung pa ye shes 'bar/ kun
mkhyen chos sku ba/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston gyi bar du brgyud pa yang yod do/ de lta bu'i gsang 'dus 'gos lugs dang mar lugs gnyis kyi brgyud pa bu ston
rin po che nas gtso cher phyogs gcig tu byung bas/ de ltar du brjod na bu ston rin po ches sras kyi thu bo khyung po lhas pa mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams la gsang ba 'dus
pa la sogs pa gdams pa thams cad gnang bas/ mar 'gos gnyis ka'i dbang bshad gdams pa dang bcas pa bum pa gang byo'i tshul du bzhugs pa yin la/ mkhas grub chen po de nyid
dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa lnga bzhes pa'i tshe/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis 'dus pa'i 'grel chen/ 'grel bshad mtha' drug rab gsal/ dbang bka'/ brgyud pa mang po'i
bka' babs phyogs gcig tu dril ba dang / sgrub thabs dang rgya gzhung mang po'i bshad pa/ rim lnga 'gos lugs sgom khrid dang bcas par rgyas par gsan/ dam pa de nyid kyi drung
du ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' bzang pos

rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa lan gsum dang / dbang bka' sgrub thabs kyi bshad pa lan mang po dang bcas pa gsan zhing / 'gos lugs kyi rim lnga'i khrid dang / mar lugs kyi rim lnga'i
khrid de gnyis ni/ bu ston nas bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI sogs brgyud de gsan pa yin la/ de lta bu'i rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mkhas
grub kyi bla ma gnyis las/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mar 'gos gnyis kyi gdams pa ma lus pa gsan nas ngor e waM chos ldan du yang nyi ma re la yang rgyud man ngag gi chos thun
gnyis re gnang ba sogs dka' spyad dang ngal dub du ma zhig dang du bzhes te/ bstan pa'i khur chen po bsnams te 'chad nyan gyis gtan la phab pas gsung rgyun zin nges pa'i
mkhas pa yang mang du byung ste/ mkhas pa'i dbang po gung ru shes rab bzang pos ngor chen gyi gsung ji ltar ba bzhin bri bar mdzad pa'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i bskyed rim gyi
rnam bshad rmongs pa'i mun sel lam/ yid kyi mun sel zhes kyang bya/ log rtog gi mun pa sel ba padmo'i gnyen zhes kyang bya ba dang / sdom brtson dam pa dpal gyi rgyal
mtshan gyis/ rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rgyun bzhin bris pa'i gsang 'dus kyi rnam bshad blo'i padmo rgyas byed ces pa dang / chos kyi rje srad pa kun blo'i gsang 'dus kyi rgyud
kyi spyi rnam chen mo sogs dang / gzhan yang sbyar byang gsal kha med pa'i ngor chen kun dga' bzang po'i gsang 'dus kyi rgyud dang man ngag gi yig cha mang po zhig kho
bo cag gis kyang mthong zhing / gzhan yang mang du yod par snang la/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi mdzad pa'i gsang ba

'dus pa'i bshad skor la/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs rgya mtsho/ sgrub thabs dngos grub rgya mtsho/ dkyil chog ye shes rgya mtsho/ mchod 'phreng
mchod sprin rgya mtsho/ gtor chog 'dod dgu'i rgya mtsho/ sbyin sreg 'phrin las rgya mtsho/ rab gnas bkra shis rgya mtsho/ bkra shis dge legs rgya mtsho sogs rgya mtsho
skor brgyad dam/ yang rdo rje sems dpa'i mchod chog dang rgya mtsho skor dgur grags pa rnams mdzad la/ gzhan yang rim lnga'i khrid yig zung 'jug gsal ba sogs yig skor
mang du mdzad nas dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bstan pa nam langs pa la nyi ma shar pa ltar gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /de'i drung du gsang 'dus 'gos lugs mar lugs gnyis ka'i chos
skor yongs su rdzogs pa gsan pa'i slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung ba'i nang nas brgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan te/
de nyid kyis gsang 'dus mar 'gos gnyis char gyi lugs legs par gsan zhing / 'chad nyan kyang yang yang mdzad pas/ mang mkhar ba brgyud 'dzin blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi rim
lnga'i khrid kyi zin bris sogs gsung rgyun bris pa'i yig cha yang mang du byung ba yin no/ /mus chen sems dpa' chen po 'di nyid la 'dus pa'i brgyud pa 'dzin pa'i slob
ma dpag tu med pa zhig byung yang / gtso bor gyur pa ni rje btsun kyi thugs kyi sras mchog kun mkhyen mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng ge ste rje 'dis sems dpa' chen po'i
drung du 'dus pa 'phags lugs dang ye shes

zhabs lugs sogs kyi dbang dang / khrid bka' bshad bka' lung bka' thams cad rdzogs par gsan/ yig cha yang 'phags skor la rim lnga'i khrid yig zung 'jug gsal ba'i kha skong dang
/ ye shes zhabs lugs 'di sa skya pa rang gi yab chos thun mong ma yin pa yin pa la dgongs nas ches cher dar ba'i thugs bzhed kyis 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i sgrub
thabs kun tu bzang po'i nyi 'od dang / de'i dkyil chog gtor chog mchod 'phreng / sgrub thabs kyi rnam bshad lam bzang gsal ba'i snang ba zhes bya ba rnams mdzad de/ 'dus
pa spyi dang / khyad par ye shes zhabs lugs mchog tu dar bar mdzad do/ /kun mkhyen chen po de nyid la 'dus pa'i chos skor nos pa'i slob ma mang du byung yang brgyud 'dzin
gyi gtso bo ni sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po mus chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen dang / paN chen kong ston dbang phyug grub pa sogs te/ rje 'jam dbyangs
sangs rgyas rin chen gyi drung du sa lo chen pos 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang bka' sogs gsan zhing / sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa la rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon
mchog lhun grub dang / nyan chen grags pa blo gros sogs 'dus pa'i chos skor gsan pa'i slob ma mang du 'phel ba'i nang nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi drung du snyigs dus
kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos 'dus pa'i chos skor sogs
zab cing rgya che ba'i chos tshul mtha' yas pa zhig gsan/ 'dus pa 'phags

lugs la sgrub thabs gzhan phan don yod/ dkyil chog gzhan phan rgyas byed/ dbang chog gzhan phan lhun grub ste gzhan phan skor gsum la sogs pa mdzad de/ dpal sa skya'i chos
grwa chen po 'di nyid du 'khon ston chen po dkon mchog rgyal po yab sras kyi dus dran gyi mchod 'bul du dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa dang / 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub
mchod lo re mos kyis 'dzugs par mdzad de/ deng sang gi bar du rgyun ma chad par phyag len rnam par dag pas brgyan te dar rgyas su bzhugs so/ /sngags 'chang bstan pa'i nyi
ma chen po nyid kyi drung du kho bo cag gi 'dren pa dam pa khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rigs ldan 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched gnyis kyis 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang bka'
sogs gsang 'dus kyi chos skor phal cher gsan zhing / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du rigs thams cad
kyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang dang dbyer ma mchis pa rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang
bka' lan 'ga' gsan zhing / yab rje bka' drin can de nyid kyi drung du slob bu'i tha chung bdag gis rang lo bcu bzhi lon dus dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang bka'/
bka' babs bdun ldan gyi smin byed gyi bdud rtsi legs par thob pa'i skal ba mchog dang ldan par gyur pa lags so/ /yang ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi drung du mus chen
dkon mchog rgya mtshos gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor rnams gsan zhing / spyan snga 'jam dbyangs de

nyid las/ bdag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid kyis gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor rdzogs
par gsan pa yin no/ /de rnams kyis mar lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas mar lugs ji ltar dar ba'i tshul bstan zin pa yin la/ gsum pa sa lugs kyi
bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas sa lugs ji ltar dar ba'i tshul la yang / sa lugs rnying ma'i brgyud pa'i rim pa dang / gsar ma'i brgyud pa'i rim pa bstan
pa'i sgo nas lugs 'di ji ltar dar ba'i tshul gnyis las/ dang po ni rje 'gos lo chen pos mkhon dkon mchog rgyal po la gnang / des skyu ra a skyabs la/ des sa chen la gnang
zhing / yang 'gos kyi slob ma rgyud kyi ka ba tshugs pa bzhi'i nang tshan dbus pa dge ser gyis gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan la 'dus pa'i dbang rgyud gdams pa mtha'
dag gnang ste/ kha'u pa la 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs bstan pa'i nor rdzas bya ba sogs dang / gzhan yang man ngag mang du bzhugs/ de nyid kyi drung du rje btsun sa skya pa
chen po kun dga' snying pos spyir mdo sngags kyi chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsan zhing / dang po bla chen 'di kha ba can gyi 'gro ba yongs kyi bsod nams kyi mgron
du 'byon pa'i rten 'brel yang bla ma 'di nyid kyis sgrig par mdzad/ bla chen 'di la sras kyi thu bo bzhi dang / dpal chen 'od po la sras gnyis byon pa'i chung ba zangs
tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan la sras che ba chos rgyal 'phags pa dang / 'gro mgon

phyag na gnyis/ chung ba slob dpon rin chen rgyal mtshan dang / ye 'byung gnyis te bzhi byon pa'i nang nas sa chen gyi sras bzhi/ chos rje khu dbon gnyis/ zangs tsha ste 'jam
dbyangs bdun brgyud dang / yang ye 'byung gi sras bdag nyid chen po nas sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che zam ma chad pa byon nas 'gro ba mang po'i don mdzad pa 'di
yang / bla ma gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'di kho na'i bka' drin yin te/ de yang bla ma sgyi chu ba gshegs pa'i zhal chems la/ sa chen la khyed rab tu byung la 'khon
tsho'i sde 'di khyongs gsungs pa bzhin bla chen gyis ser chas bsgrubs nas rab tu byung bar brtsams pas/ de nyid bla ma gnam kha'u pas dgongs nas/ bla chen la nga'i drung
du shog gsungs pa byung nas byon pa na/ khyed ser chas bsgrubs nas ci byed gsungs/ rab tu 'byung ba lags zhus pas/ ma byed gsungs bla ma sgyi chu ba'i gsung yin zhus
pas/ bla ma mnyam po la khong shi bo'i gsung las/ nga gson po'i ngag la nyon rab tu ma byung na phan che ba yong gsungs nas ma gnang bar brten/ de nas bla chen 'dis slar
gdung sras spel ba la brten/ 'jam dbyangs bdun brgyud sogs bar ma chad par byon nas sa skya pa zhes pa'i snyan grags srid pa gsum na cher gsal zhing kha ba can gyi skye
dgu mtha' dag smin grol la bkod de/ 'dzam gling byang phyogs 'dir rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pa'i dge legs kyi rgyun 'di bzhin byung ba yin no/ /de lta
bu'i bla ma gnam kha'u pa'i drung du rje btsun 'dis mtshan nyid skor la byams chos sogs mang po dang / sngags la

bya rgyud rig pa mchog gi rgyud/ legs grub/ dpung bzang / gsang ba spyi rgyud/ bsam gtan phyi ma'i rgyud sogs 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa/ spyod rgyud la rnam snang mngon
byang 'grel pa phran dang bcas pa/ yo ga la de nyid 'dus pa'i rgyud 'grel bcas/ dpal mchog dang po'i rgyud/ rdo rje rtse mo sogs 'grel pa dang bcas pa mang po dang / bla
med la 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dbang / dgongs 'grel gyi bstan bcos sgron gsal/ mdo bsre/ mdo byas/ rim lnga spyod bsdus/ bdag byin gyis rlabs pa'i rim pa/ sems kyi sgrib
sbyong / dkyil chog nyi shu pa/ zla grags kyi rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs sogs 'dus pa 'phags skor gyi gzhung gdams ngag dang bcas pa mang po zhig dang / ye shes zhabs
lugs kyi sgrub thabs kun bzang 'grel pa gsum dang bcas pa sogs 'dus pa lugs gnyis kyi gdams pa phal cher ba gsan pa yin la/ de nyid kyis gnam kha'ub pa rdo rje bdud 'joms
la/ des rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan la gnang ba yin la/ yang lo rgyus kyi yi ge 'ga' zhig las/ sa chen gyis slob dpon rin po che la gnang / des rje btsun
la gnang ba yin gsungs nas/ rdo rje bdud 'joms ma bgrangs pa yang yod la/ gang ltar rje btsun rin po che nas bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bla
chen 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ brag phug pa blo brtan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang
po sogs kyi bar du brgyud nas de man chad gong mar

'gos gnyis kyi brgyud rim dang phal cher 'dra ba yin no/ /gnyis pa gsar ma'i brgyud rim bstan pa'i sgo nas lugs de ji ltar dar ba'i tshul ni/ kha che'i paNDa ིta chen po shAkya
shrI bha dra bod du byon pa'i legs lam la brten nas byung ba yin te/ de yang spyir paN chen 'di kha che khri brtan gyi bye brag dza shwa dha ra zhes par shing mo glang
gi lo bltams/ dgung lo bcu pa la bram ze lakShindha ra la sgra rig pa gsan/ lo dgu pa la dge bsnyen bsgrubs nas nyer gnyis kyi bar du tshangs spyod kyi dge bsnyen mdzad/
nyer gsum pa la mkhan po su kha shrI bha dra ste bde ba dpal bzang po la rab byung zhus nas nyer dgu'i bar du kha cher bzhugs shing / sum cu pa la yul dbus ma ga dhAr
byon te mkhan po shanta ka ra gupta zhi ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pa dang / da sha bha la dang / gsang ston dha bar sogs dge slong bco brgyad las bsnyen par rdzogs pa mdzad nas
'phags yul nyid du sbyangs pa cher mdzad pas/ mdo sngags rig gnas dang bcas pa sogs shes bya thams cad la mkhas pa'i pha rol tu son te/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa ches cher gsal
bar mdzad pa'i rigs nas dgung lo drug cu bzhes pa'i dus khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal dgung lo so gsum lon pa'i tshe/ paN chen 'di bod du spyan 'dren par byon te
rgya gar bairYa'i tshong dus su phebs pas/ ba ne shA ra bya bar paN chen dang mjal ba na/ paN chen gyi gsung gis/ lo tsA ba 'di chos mang du shes pa lha chen bzhengs pa'i
stobs yod pa'i yar rgan zhig yod bsam pa la na tshod gzhon nur 'dug chos bsgyur ba'i lo tsA yang mi phod/ sgrub thabs 'ga' byin la 'o skol dpon slob phyir bzlog gsungs/

paNDi ta dza ya shrIs dpon slob rnams lo tsA ba'i gzugs la brnyas 'dug pas 'bel ba'i gtam smros shig ces lo tsA ba la skabs dbye ba na/ lo tsA bas paN chung dgu la dri ba mi
'dra ba gnyis gnyis byas pas/ paN chen mnyes te spyan drangs ba'i rngo thogs nas/ kha che'i paNDi ta chen po de 'khor paN chung dgu dang bcas pa bod du rim gyis spyan drangs
chu mig tu phebs pa na/ khro phu bas bsu ba'i bkod pa dge 'dun drug cu/ dar gdugs rol mo sogs drug cu dang bcas pa slebs/ khro phur gdan drangs/ de'i tshe sa skya paNDi
ta'i yab dpal chen 'od po sku gshegs pa'i gshegs rdzong gi sku skal rkyang 'dur du 'bul bar phebs pa'i bar lam chu mig tu paN chen dang thog mar mjal/ tshad ma chos
mchog gi bstod pa sogs mdzad pa yin zer/ gang ltar de nas paN chen gyis khro phur byi lo'i dbyar gnas mdzad pa'i tshe tshul shing len pa brgyad brgya byung bar grags shing
/ brgyad stong pa la sogs tshogs chos gsungs/ lo tsA bas dar zab kyi thun yon re ma chag par phul/ lho brag pa byang chub dpal bsnyen rdzogs gnang / de nas 'bri khung pas
spyan 'dren pa'i cha rkyen mang po slebs/ slas mo cher phebs te rgya gar nas spyan drangs pa'i rten mchod rnams zhal phye mchod pa zab par phul/ de dus gtsang po ba bsod
nams mdzes kyis zhal mjal te/ bdag bsnyen par rdzogs nas ltung ba byung ba mi dran pas tshul khrims bsrung ba'i dge ba bsngo bar zhus pas/ paN chen gyis dbu zhwa zul gyis
phud phyag thal mo sbyar nas bsngo rgyu bzang 'di lta bu rgya gar na yang dkon gsungs nas bsngo ba rgyas par mdzad/ glang lo'i dbyar gnas kyang slas mo

cher mdzad de dgag dbye thon nas chu mig ring mor byon/ rgyan gong gnas su rdo rje dpal la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / de nas gzhu snying mo'i nang la byon tshur phu nas stod lung
brgyud jo bo rnam gnyis la mchod pa phul/ mtshur phu ba'i skyel mi rnams la khyed kyi dgon pa na sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud nas bshad pa'i sku gsum snang ba khyed kyis
ngo ma shes gsungs/ sku gsum ni bde mchog yab yum go ldog shAkya thub pa sprul sku la yum rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ rdo rje dril bu mnyam sbyor gyi lha dang gsum mo/ /de nas srin
po rir stag lo'i dbyar gnas mdzad/ byams chos lnga dang khri rigs tshogs rnams gsungs/ me mo yos la sol nag thang po cher phebs te bstan rtsis mdzad pa na/ smin drug
zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi tshes brgyad nam gung mnyam pa la/ zla ba ri bo ma nub tshe/ /thub dbang yongs su mya ngan 'das/ /der rjes lo ni stong phrag gcig /bdun brgya dang
ni lnga bcu dang / /zla ba gnyis dang zla ba phyed/ /de bzhin nyi ma snga rab 'das/ /zhes sogs bshad do/ /de nas byang rwa sgreng du byon pa'i yar lam 'bri khung pas spyan
drangs kyang / gdan gcig pa dang bka' gdams pas gegs byas mjal du ma ster zhes kyang grags/ phyi de sa pho 'brug gi lo gtsang du phebs/ nyang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug
lag khang du bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDa ta chen po la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / de'i tshe dgung lo re lnga pa yin zhing / sbrul lo'i dbyar gnas rin chen sgang du mdzad
de/ rta lo'i dbyar gnas shong lu gu gdong du mdzad de/ lha btsun gung thang pa la bsnyen rdzogs gnang nas/ spre'u lo slar yang khro phur phebs te

spre'u lo'i dbyar gnas kyang gnas der mdzad/ lhag par chu pho spre'u lo bre zla ba'i tshes gsum nas bcu gsum gyi bar la khro phu byams chen la rab gnas mdzad cing / rim gyis
khro phu nas mnga' ris su phebs/ bya lo'i dbyar gnas pu hrang du mdzad/ shing pho khyi lo kha cher phebs te/ bod du lo bcu gcig bzhugs/ bstan 'gro'i don dpag med mdzad
pas mdo sngags gnyis ka'i bstan pa la phan shin tu che/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / byang rdor gnyis ka bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa dang / shong pa jo gdan
dang / seng ge zil gnon la me tog phreng rgyud sogs rgyas par gnang ste/ 'dul ba stod lugs smad lugs gnyis kyi steng du/ 'dul ba'i brgyud pa zur pa zhig kyang spel ba yin
la/ de'i nang nas byang rdor gnyis kyis dge 'dun gyi sde so sor btsugs pa ni/ dge 'dun sgang pa dang / tshogs mo che ba ste/ de gnyis las mched pa la bye ma rdzing bu
pa dang / chos lung pa zhes grags te de bzhi la jo gdan tshogs sde bzhi zhes deng sang yang grags pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i paN chen de la slob ma mang du byung yang / sa skya
paNDi ta kho na sras kyi dam par mdzad pa yin te/ paN chen 'dis bdag nyid chen po la bod rgan po'i 'dres kyis ma bslad pa'i lha rgyan gyi bshad srol las byon pa'i tshad
ma'i gzhung lugs kyi gtso bo chos kyi grags pa'i rnam 'grel dang / gzhan yang dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang sogs zab mo sngags phyogs mang po dang / lhag par gser zho brgya
dang / g.yu zho brgya ri ba gcig rnams phul nas ma hA paNDi tas srung ma rnams kyi nang nas thugs gtsigs

su mdzad pa'i gsang sgrub cig yod 'dug pa/ de bdag la cis kyang gnang dgos zhus pas/ 'di lta bu ngas sngar rgya bod du slob ma su la yang ster ma phod pa yin na'ang / khyed
sa skya pa chos skyong 'di'i bdag por 'os pa 'dug pas de bzhin byed gsungs/ gzhan yang gdams pa 'di zhu ba byung dogs pas/ rgya skad du bya'o gsungs nas gnang / chos rje
pas kyang rgya yig tu bris/ phyis mchod rten khru gang ba gcig gi nang du bcug nas zhabs sdom bsdams nas rten gyi gral na yod pa na/ slob ma bgres po kyai rdo rje zhal lan
gsum gzigs pa'i dge slong zla ba rgyal mtshan bya ba lo bdun cu lon pa gcig gis chos skyong gi lung bstan byung nas/ spyad dngos thams cad spangs thag byas nas phul te
'di zhus nas gnang / khong gis bsnyen pa byas pa tsam gyis khong gi zhing la rkun ma byung ba la/ rkun ma lnga zhag gcig la khrag skyugs nas shi ba sogs nus mthu dpag med
byung / de lta bu gdams pa de la paN chen gyi zhal nas rang la ci ri ba 'di la ri ba yin/ bod du 'di las zab pa'i chos skyong gi gdams pa yongs myong ba med ces gsungs
pas che brjod kyang dpag med mdzad pa yin la/ khyad par dus der gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang dang rgyud sgrub thabs gdams pa kun cha tshang bar gsan/ de'i tshe lo paN khyad par
can kha che paN chen dang / bdag nyid chen po sa paN gnyis kyis klu byang gi dkyil chog nyi shu pa dang / sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog zung
'jug gsal ba gnyis gsar du bsgyur/ de phyin chad nas sngar gyi dbang bka' la rnying pa dang /

kha che paN chen nas brgyud pa'i klu byang gi dkyil chog nyi shu pa gsar du bsgyur ba de'i lugs kyi dbang bka' la dbang bka' gsar ma'i tha snyad kyang grags pa yin no/ /des
na bdag nyid chen po sa paN la gsang 'dus 'gos lugs/ mar lugs/ kha che paN chen gyi lugs dang gsum bzhugs pa yin te/ 'gos lugs gsan tshul gong du bstan zin la/ mar lugs
ni 'khon gad pa kIrti sogs nas brgyud pa'i rim lnga stan thog gcig ma sogs gsan pa yin te/ rab dbyer chos gsan tshul 'chad pa'i skabs su/ rim lnga stan thog gcig ma dang
/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan rang nyid kyis rtogs pa'i brgyud 'dzin tshogs grub dbon gsum gyi dbon po chos
kyi rgyal po 'phags pa dang / 'od zer shAkya gnyis la gnang zhing / chos rgyal 'phags pas lugs 'di'i dkyil chog kyang mdzad de zhing dkon mchog dpal ba la gnang / de nyid
nas ngor chen kun dga' bzang po'i bar dbang bka' rnying ma'i brgyud pa dang 'dra la/ yang 'od zer shAkyas kyang lugs 'di'i sgrub thabs shig mdzad cing / de nyid kyis kha'u
pa dar ma shes rab la gnang / des se mor pa rin chen dpal bya ba la/ des bla ma rwa gnyis pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ des chos rgyal 'phags pa'i slob ma spro lung pa kun
dga' smon lam la gnang / 'dis kyang 'dus pa sa lugs kyi sgrub thabs mdzad cing / de nyid kyis bla ma don rin grags chen la gnang / de nas 'phags 'od sogs gong mar 'gos
gnyis kyi skabs su bstan pa ltar yin no/ /de ltar 'dus pa'i chos skor rgya mtsho lta bu'i nang nas rang

nyid kyis nos pa'i tshul mdo tsam zhig brjod na/ gsang 'dus lugs gsum gyi mi bskyod rdo rje'i smin byed kyi dbang ni yab rje chos kyi rgyal po las nos pa'i tshul gong du bstan
pa ltar dang / 'dus pa spyan ras gzigs dang / 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dbang ni/ rgyal ba mus pa chen po nas brgyud pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du nos pa'i tshul
'og nas 'byung ba ltar yin la/ bskyed rim gyi bshad pa dang / rdzogs rim zab mo rim lnga'i khrid/ rgyud rgyud 'grel dang bcas pa gzhan yang rgya bod kyi gzhung rnams
kyi bshad lung sogs 'dus pa'i chos skor zab cing rgya che ba phal che ba rnams ni/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi zhal
snga nas kyang bka' drin las nye bar nos pa yin te/ de yang kho bo cag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa buddha'i mtshan can nyid kyis spyan snga 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog rgya
mtsho'i drung du/ kun mkhyen gyi slob ma rje sangs rgyas rin chen dang / paN chen dbang phyug grub pa gnyis kyi dngos slob bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug las brgyud pa'i rim
lnga 'gos lugs dang mar lugs gnyis ka'i khrid/ dbang rgyud man ngag 'grel pa 'grel bshad dang bcas pa bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan zhing mnyes pa gsum gyi sgo nas mnyes
par mdzad de/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho nyid kyis ci gsungs pa'i bka' thams cad dang du bzhes pa la brten/ rten 'brel thams cad rang 'grig tu gyur te/ 'phrin las kyis
rgya mtsho'i gos can du khyab pa'i legs tshogs thams cad lhun grub tu 'byung ba yin te/ de yang bdag gi rnam 'dren dam pa rje btsun

mus pa chen po 'di nyid kyis bla med kyi dbang gis gzhan don mdzad pa'i thog ma yang gsang ba 'dus pa'i mi bskyod pa'i dbang gis gzhan phan 'phrin las kyi sgo dang po phye
ba yin te/ de'i tshul yang sngon rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho gling dga' bde ba can du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig gsang 'dus kyi chos skor don gnyer gyi slob bu che btsun mang po
zhig phyogs nas 'dus pa'i tshe/ rje spyan snga 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gsung gis/ da lam gyi gsang 'dus don gnyer 'dir 'dus pa rnams la chos rje shangs pas dbang bskur gyis/
de nas nged kyis khrid sogs ston pa yin no zhes gsungs pa'i bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i sta gon gyi nub mo rje nyid kyi mnal lam du/ dkon mchog gi rten gyi drung du zan ril
brtag pa zhig mdzad kyin 'dug pa na/ ril bu gcig phyir 'thon pa la me 'bar nas je mtho je mthor song ste mthar nam mkha'i dbyings su thim pa'i mtshan ltas gsal bar byung
gsungs/ 'di ni rje btsun bla ma nyid kyi 'phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam pas gdul bya rnams mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su 'dren nus pa'i mtshan ma yang
dag pa yin par nges so/ /dus de tsam nas bzung rje nyid dgung lo bdun cu don bdun bzhes pa tsam gyi bar la bgrang ba las 'das pa'i gdul bya rnams la/ spyir mdo sngags kyi
chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dang / khyad par dpal ldan gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba dang / zab mo rim lnga'i khrid ston
pa dang / de dag gi rgyab rten rgyud rgyud 'grel dang bcas pa'i bshad bka' sogs kyi sgo nas pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa'i bstan

pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel zhing rgyas par mdzad cing / lhag pa'i lha 'di nyid kyi bskyed rdzogs zab mo'i rnal 'byor dang / gsang sngags kyi bzlas brjod rnams kyang ji
srid mtshan ma brnyes kyi bar du thugs nyams su bzhes pa la brten/ zhing skyong tsa turmu kha 'di nyid rje nyid kyi bran bzhin du bka' nyan cing 'phrin las sgrub pa'i ngo
mtshar ba'i rnam thar mang du yod de/ de yang rje 'di sa skyar phebs pa'i skabs shig gdan sa'i mgon khang gong 'og dang / kha'u skyed lhas sogs su gnas mjal mdzad dus kha'u
brag rdzong du nyi ma gsum gyi bar la mchod gtor rgya chen po mdzad pas/ de'i nyi ma dang po'i nyin gtor tshogs kyi steng gi nam mkha' la ral gri me 'bar ba zhig 'dug
pa mngon sum du gzigs shing / nyi ma bar ma'i nyin 'phags pa brag phug na thugs dam la bzhugs dus/ bar snang la bram ze dkar po zhig phar 'gro tshur 'gro byed pa mngon sum
du gzigs zhes rje nyid kyi gsung las thos shing / chos skyong bram ze'i gzugs can nyid mngon sum du gzigs pa'i skabs der gzhan yang gzigs snang khyad par can du ma byung
bar nges la/ zhing skyong chen po 'di sa skya pa'i chos skyong gzhan rnams las kyang rje nyid la lhag par 'go bas/ bdag gi bla ma 'di dang mi la mi lab pa'i tshul gyis
bran bzhin du 'khol ba'i rnam thar mang du yod kyang / kho bos rje 'di'i rnam thar logs su bkod pa rnams su thun mong du brjod rung ba rnams ni rgyas par bris zin cing /
thun mong ma yin pa dag ni chos skyong gnyan pas bri bar ma nus so/ /de ltar zhing skyong chen po 'di rje bla ma

'di la chos skyong gzhan las 'go ba yang / zhing skyong 'di gtso bor gsang ba 'dus pa'i bstan bsrung yin pas/ rje 'di 'dus pa'i bstan 'dzin bla na med pa yin pa'i gtan tshigs
yang dag pa yin la de lta bu'i bdag gi bla ma dam pa yongs 'dzin 'brel tshad don ldan 'di nyid kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa rgyas pa ni don tshan bcu gsum gyi
sgo nas zhib tu bstan pa'i rje 'di'i rtogs brjod rgyas pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba dang / 'bring po byin rlabs dgos 'dod kun 'byung bya ba dang / bsdus
pa ngo mtshar utpa la'i chun po rnams su legs par bshad pa las khongs su chud par bya'o/ /de ltar yongs 'dzin dam pa de nyid kyis kho bo cag la zab rgyas kyi dam pa'i
chos kyi bka' drin tshad med pas bskyangs shing / thugs rje'i spyan ras kyis bu gcig pa'i ma bzhin rjes su bzung ba la brten/ rje de nyid dus gsum gyi rgyal ba kun gyi spro
bsdu'i byed por nges pa'i shes pa snying nas rnyed de/ 'di phyi'i don thams cad mgon po de nyid kyi thugs rje las gzhan du re ba'i yid gnyis cung zad kyang med pa'i gang
byung gcig chog rgyal po bla ma'i thugs rje dang byin rlabs las byung bar blo thag chod pa 'di yang 'dren pa dam pa gang gi byin rlabs snying la zhugs pa'i dge mtshan
las byung ba yin no/ /de yang kho bo cag rje 'di dang mjal ba'i tshul ni rang nyid lo gzhon nu'i dus grub thob gong ma'i rnam thar 'ga' zhig mthong ba'i rkyen byas nam 'chi
cha med kyi tshe thung 'di la tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa zhig bya snyam pa dang / yang na 'chad nyan dang / thugs dam spel mar byas te/ mi tshe stong zad du ma song ba
zhig cis kyang bya snyam

pa dang / de dag gang byed kyang bla ma mtshan nyid dang ldan pa zhig dang ma mjal na thabs mi 'dug snyam pa sogs chos kyi snang ba mi chung tsam yod cing / lhag par rje btsun
bslu med dam pa nyid kyi rnam par thar pa cung zad thos pa'i mod la snying nas mjal 'dod kyi 'dun pa kha zhe med pa yang yang skyes pa dang / rje 'di la chos thob pa
dang sku drung nas 'ong ba yin zer ba rnams dang 'phrad dus khyed rnams re dga' bla ma sangs rgyas de lta bu dang mjal 'dug snyam pa dang / lhag par 'jam pa'i dbyangs mthu
stobs dbang phyug rje 'di'i zhabs drung du rab byung dang / dbang rjes gnang mang po zhus nas phebs byung skabs/ rje 'di'i rnam thar 'dra gsungs byung pas/ bdag kyang rje
dang mjal nas chos thob pa zhig byung na dga' ba la zhus shing / snying nas kyang mjal 'dod lhang lhang je 'phel du song ba zhig byung / yang rje nyid ngam ring du phebs
skabs shig sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang gnang ba grub nas/ rtsa brgyad pa 'tsho byed lha 'byor gdan sa chen por sleb byung ba'i lag par dpung skud cig 'dug pa la/
khyed kyis nye stabs dbang su la zhus smras pas/ rje mus chen la sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang thob pa yin zer zhing / rje'i rnam thar 'ga' zhig 'phros byung bas/ nged
kyang bla ma sangs rgyas de dang mjal nas chos thob pa'i dus shig e yong na zhes pa ngag nas kyang shor zhing yid la yang byung ba yin la/ de nas skabs shig bdag la bka'
drin mchog tu che ba'i ma cig lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo de nyid ngam ring du mi dbang chen po mjal ba la phebs pa'i sgo dod song ba na/

der skabs rje mus chen nyid kyang ngam ring na bzhugs so zhes thos byung bas bdag gi bsam pa la da lta gangs can gyi khrod na dge ba'i bshes gnyen thos bsam sgom gsum mthar
phyin nas/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan ma lus pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur cing / lhag par dad ldan gyi slob bu la mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub bde blag tu stsol
zhing / mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga' ba'i skyes bu rje mus chen kho na las gzhan med do zhes dpyod ldan gzur gnas mang po'i ngag las thos shing / rang yang snying
nas yid ches pa la brten/ da ni kho bo cag 'di phyi bar do gsum gyi skyabs gnas dang 'dren pa zhu ba'i blo rtse'i gtad mtshams kyi yul sngar gyi bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs
sku mched zhal rnam pa gnyis dang / rje bla ma 'di kho na las gzhan med par rtogs nas bka' drin can gyi ma gcig lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo brgyud pa'i bdag gis rje 'di
la zhu yig phul ba'i don 'bras la/ bdag tshe ha cang mi ring ba zhig byung na thos bsam rgya cher byas pa la don mi 'dug pas tshe ring thung 'ong dang / thog ma mdo sngags
gang la sbyang na legs dang / dbu zhwa sogs sku dreg phog nges pa'i na bza' zhig byin rlabs rten du gnang ba dang / sems la phan pa'i gsung mgur bslab ston zhig gnang
dgos zhus pas/ de'i lan du thugs dam gsung shog 'di bzhin gnang byung ste/ 'jam dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs drung
du zhu ba/ sku gsung thugs rab tu dwangs shing dkar phyogs dge ba la mngon par brtson pa'i skabs/ thugs dam bka' shog

dam rdzas kyi gnang sbyin dang bcas spyi bor phebs pas bka' drin che lags/ sku phywa btab pas sku tshe ring po yong bar gda'/ thugs sbyong sngon ma gang mdzad pa dga' btab
pas mdo mdzad pa dga' bar gda'/ thugs sbyong mdzad gong mi g.yo ba dkar po'i bsnyen pa zhig gnang na dga' ba gda' lags/ thugs dam slob gnyer la sogs pa mdzad na'ang thugs
rtse dkon mchog la gtad/ nges 'byung drag po'i sgo nas rgyud bskul/ sems can thams cad kyi don du sangs rgyas thob 'dod kyis bsam pas mdzad dgos te/ rje sa paN gyis/ mdor
na chos kyi ci byed som/ /sangs rgyas byed na chos bzhin gyis/ /zhes gsungs/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i nyams su len pa'i chos la/ blo snying brang gsum gtad nas/ /sems
snang chos su bsres shig /'di phyi bar do gsum du/ /'di yi bslu ba med pas/ /ma nor lam la 'bungs shig /ces gsungs pa sogs mang dag gda' na'ang yi ge mang dogs ma bris
la/ mdor na snga mu ltar thugs dam thugs sbyong ral med/ bstan pa dgongs nas mkhyen mkhyen/ zhu yig gzigs rten tshe mdud la rgya mdzes phul/ zhwa mo sogs bdag gi dri phog
pas 'bul ma nus zhes gsungs pa 'dug pa mthong ba'i mod la/ rje de nyid la mjal 'dod dang chos thob 'dod kyi blo me 'bar ba la shing bsnan pa ltar je 'phel du gyur pa zhig
byung la/ de nas dus ha cang mi ring ba zhig lon pa glang lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nub/ bdag gi bka' drin can gyi yum de nyid glo

bur du gshegs pa la brten/ yid la bzod thabs med pa'i zug rngu drag pos kun tu gzir zhing / gang la yang snying po med par rtogs pa'i nges 'byung drag pos tshe 'di blos gtang
gi sgrub pa zhig byed 'dod nas/ snga gong zhig rje btsun gyi sku 'dra mdze thod ma'i drung du mchod pa rgya chen dang bcas gsol ba btab nas lung bstan zhus pa la/ 'brel
tshad don ldan gyi bla ma rje mus chen nyid dang mjal ba zhig 'ong mi 'ong dang / tshe 'di blos gtang gi sgrub pa zhig byas na bar snang la 'phur nus pa'i grub thob cig
'ong mi 'ong dang / yang tshe 'dir bshad sgrub spel mar byas na bar dor 'bras bu 'grub pa zhig 'ong mi 'ong rnams lung bstan zhus pas/ lung bstan mi bzang ba ma byung zhing
/ de mthun gyi ma gcig lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshul bstan ma thag pa'i skabs der/ rje nyid kyi drung du lam ston gyi chas rnams phul ba
dang bcas zhu yig phul ba'i don 'bras la sngar rje btsun gyi sku brnyan drung du lung bstan zhus pa'i rnam grangs rnams dang / lhag par bka' drin can gyi yum de gang du
'khrungs yod rnams lung bstan gsal kha can zhig dgos tshul zhus pa na/ de'i lan du thugs dam gsung shog 'di bzhin gnang byung ste/ 'jam dbyangs rin po che'i zhabs drung
du zhu ba/ sku'i dkyil 'khor mngon par mtho zhing thos bsam sgom gsum la thugs brtson par bzhugs skabs nas/ gsung shog gos gser ma dang bcas gnang ba thugs la btags/ yum
rin po che cho 'phrul gyi tshes bco lnga la sku tshe'i tshad rdzogs pa ltar mdzad nas gshegs pa de bya ba kham can byung 'dug lags kyang / 'di ltar skyes pa thams

cad kyi/ /mdun na 'dug pa 'chi ba yin/ /zhes dang / mtshan dang dpe byad brgyan pa yi/ /rdo rje'i sku yang mi rtag na/ /chu shing snying po med 'dra ba'i/ /chu lbur 'dus la
smos ci dgos/ /zhes pa la sogs pa gsungs pa ltar 'dus byas thams cad mi rtag par gda' ba/ yin lugs kyang kun rdzob tu chos thams cad rmi lam sgyu ma lta bu dang / don dam
par spros bral yin par thugs la bzhugs par zhu lags/ lung bstan byed pa la sa dang po chos nyid kyi bden pa mthong dgos mod/ bdag lta bu de'i phyed dang po tsam gyi yon
tan gang yang med pas lung bstan ga la yong lags/ yum de mkha' 'gro'i mtshan rtags tshang ba dang / grongs rkyen dang grongs dus zhal ngo rnams kyi byin rlabs la brten gnas
mthon por 'khrungs pa gzhir bcas su 'dug lags/ zhabs drung rin po che rang la bshad sgrub gnyis ka la mo bzang ba rang 'dug lags/ rang re zhal mjal ba zhig yong zer ba
babs lags/ da phyin thugs dam dang / thugs gnyer spel mar gnang mdzod la/ nyams len gang mdzad dang bya ba gang mdzad thams cad dkon mchog gsum la mgo bcad pang skyur gyi
tshul du thog khel gyi rtse gcig tu thugs gtod par zhu lags/ slar sku tshe ring zhing bkra shis la thugs bsam chos bzhin du 'grub par smon lags/ sku rim srung 'khor yang
ched gtad bsgrub lags pas/ bde kye yo ga gsum gyi rgyud man ngag gzhung phran dang bcas pa rnams la gzigs rtog phul phyin rang sa ngor gnyis kyi bstan pa la thugs bzhag
pa mkhyen mkhyen/

cis kyang dgos gsungs pa nas zhu yig spyan zur g.yo rten bo dhi tsitta'i 'phreng ba la rgya mdzes phul zhes gsungs pa 'dug pa mthong bas sems dga' ba dang spro ba tshad las
'das pa rab dga'i sa thob pa ltar gyur pa yin no/ /tshul de lta bu'i sgo nas mtshams sbyar te yun ring po ma lon pa kho bo cag rang lo bcu bdun du sleb pa rje nyid dgung
gi lo bdun cu rtsa gnyis su phebs pa'i glang gi lo gling dga' bde ba can gyi chos grwa chen por rje bla ma nyid zhal mjal/ de nas bzung lo grangs du ma zhig gi bar du dad
pa dang gus pa che cher bgyis te/ dam pa de nyid kyi zhal gyi bum bzang las/ skal bzang las 'phro can bdag gis dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi ci yang zhig thob pa yin te de
yang bstan pa'i rtsa ba so sor thar pa'i sdom pa gsol bzhi'i cho ga la brten nas dge bsnyen yongs su rdzogs pa'i bar dang / sems bskyed kyi sdom pa dbu sems kyi lugs las
khyad par du 'phags pa'i brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi cho ga las legs par nos shing / rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa rgyud sde'i dgongs pa tshad ldan gyi skyes bus legs
par bkral ba'i dkyil 'khor bgrang ba las 'das pa rnams su cho ga rnam par dag pa'i sgo nas thob par mdzad de/ mdor na bstan pa'i rtsa ba sdom pa gsum po so so'i cho ga dang
/ dbang dus su gsum char thob par gsungs pa'i bka' drin nos shing / der rjes brgyud pa dri ma med pa las 'ong ba'i thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i zab khrid mi 'dra
ba lnga phrag gsum tsam dang / de dag dang 'brel ba'i rgyud rgya gzhung 'grel pa 'grel bshad dang bcas pa'i chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu'i bka' drin

stsol bar mdzad pa yin la/ de'i nang nas rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa shin tu smin pa cha lag phra mo tshun chad
rgyas shing zhib par zhus pas/ rje'i gsung las/ chos bdag po la 'phrod blo bde/ zhes gsungs pa sogs thugs dgyes pa'i gsung du ma 'byon par mdzad cing / lhag par lam 'bras
pa yongs la ma grags pa'i brda chig brgyud thun mong ma yin pa sogs mtha' chod par stsal/ gzhan yang sa skya pa'i yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril
gsum nA ro mkha' spyod dang bcas pa'i dbang byin rlabs bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid zab mo man ngag phra mo tshun/ de'i rgyab rten rgyud dang rgya bod kyi gzhung du ma'i bshad
lung sogs bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gnang zhing / khyad par du yang rje nyid dgung lo bdun cu don drug bzhes shing kho bo cag rang lo nyer gcig lon pa'i sbrul lo nag
pa zla ba la gling dga' bde ba can gyi yang dben bsam gtan phu'i gnas mchog de nyid du dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor rnams stsal ba yin te/ de yang bdag gi bla ma rje
btsun dam pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje de nyid kyi sku mthong ba tsam dang / tshul khrims kyi dri bsung tshor ma thag sku drung de nyid du blo lhing phebs shing / tha
mal gyi rtog pa rags pa rnams rang 'gags su khrig 'gro zhing / zhal gyi dkyil 'khor kho na blta ba las yid gzhan du mi 'phro ba dang / thugs lhag bsam rnam par dag cing ting
nge 'dzin bzang po'i rgyun la chos gsungs pa'i tshe yang skabs skabs su yug

re 'byams 'gro ba dang bstun nas gsung las/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos rnams las de bzhin du 'byung bas/ de bzhin du bsgoms na/ srid pa hrul por 'jig pa la tshegs med/ ces nyams
ldan gyi tshig 'ga' gsungs pa'i tshe/ de ma thag chos dang bla ma la nges shes khyad par can dbang med du skye ba dang / gsung rab la sbyangs pa med pa'i skye bo phal pa
zhig yin kyang / zhal mthong zhing gsung thos pa tsam gyis sems rnal du phebs cing mi lus thengs gcig tsam thob pa 'di don dang ldan pa byas so snyam pa'i dga' spro khyad
par can bskyed pa dang / bdag rang gi bsam pa la yang bla ma sangs rgyas mi gzugs can 'di 'dra ba'i drung du rgyud sde'i nges gsang sa skya pa'i yab chos lhad med 'di lta
bu thos shing nyams su len pa'i skal ba 'di 'dra ba a re dga' snyam pa'i dad pa dang / spro ba rang shugs kyis skye ba dang bcas rjes su bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa bka'
drin can de nyid bdag cag slob ma rnams kyi dbus der sku mdzes shing zil che la bag bro ba de drang por bsrangs nas/ zhal dkyil zla ba rgyas pa 'dra ba'i utpal lta bu'i
spyan gnyis kyis slob bu'i tshogs la dal bus gzigs shing / dpal gyi mgul nas 'phrul gyi ljags bskyangs te/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa nyid la sku tshe hril po sbyangs pa ltar
lugs 'di'i rgyas bshad don bsdu dka' gnas kyi bshad pa sogs gang mdzad kyang de kho na la sbyangs pa ltar dpyod ldan kun gyi rna bar snyan cing snying la 'bab pa'i gsung
ha cang dal ba dang / brel ba'i rkyen spangs pa'i

dag gsal snyan pa'i sgo nas nyin rang po chos kyi grwar bzhugs kyang skyo sun cung zad kyang mi skye ba'i ngang nas dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i smin byed kyi dbang
thog mar stsal zhing / de nas rim lnga 'gos lugs kyi khrid yig rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi zung 'jug gsal ba dang / rje sems dpa' chen po'i gsung la mang mkhar ba brgyud
'dzin blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis zin bris su btab pa'i yi ge gnyis kyi steng nas/ dpal ldan gsang ba 'dus pa'i zab khrid smin rgyas su stsal te/ de'i rgyab rten du rgyud
rgyud 'grel dang bcas pa dang / rgya bod kyi gzhung rnams kyi bshad pa dang lung gi tshogs kyang zhib par gnang ste/ rje btsun gang gi gsung gi bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun
gyis bdag blo'i bum pa yongs su gang bar gyur te rab dga'i sa thob pa lta bu'i dga' bde'i dpal la rang gzhan kun 'khod par mdzad pa'i bka' drin stsal ba yin no/ /'o na gong
du bstan pa'i sa lugs kyi dbang bka' gsar rnying gnyis mi 'dra ba'i khyad par ji lta bu zhe na/ bshad par bya ste/ dbang bka' gsar rnying gnyis gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod
pa'i dbang bka' 'khrul med rnam par dag pa re yin pas/ don gyi ngo bo ni mi mthun pa med la/ 'on kyang skur byed cho ga'i gzhung tha dad par yin pa dang / bod 'dir srol
'byed snga phyi cung zad byung bas/ de gnyis la gsar rnying gi brda chad sa lugs nyid la grags pa ltar don la gnas pa yin pa las/ skur byed cho ga'i gzhung tha dad pa
yin te/ snga ma ni klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i cho ga nyi shu pa la brten pa yin

zhing / phyi ma ni klu byang gis mdzad pa'i cho ga nyi shu pa dang / sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i zung 'jug gsal ba kha che paN chen dang chos rje sa paN
gnyis kyis gsar du bsgyur ba la brten pa yin pas so/ /srol 'byed kyang snga phyi so so ba yin te/ snga ma ni 'gos lo chen po de nyid kyi bka' drin las byung ba yin la/
phyi ma ni 'gos lo la ma ltos par kha che'i paNDi ta chen po ma byon sangs rgyas gsum pa shAkya shrI bha dra dang / kha ba can gyi bstan pa'i sgron me chen po 'dzam gling
mkhas pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam pa mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan bzang po gnyis kyi bka' drin las yongs su dar ba yin pas so/ /des na
de gnyis skur byed kyi cho ga mi 'dra ba'i khyad par ni lugs phyi ma 'dir 'jug pa'i skabs su lha ngo bstan pa'i rjes nyid du dkyil 'khor dang lha'i rnam dag ston pa bshad
cing phyag len la yang mdzad/ dbang dngos gzhir sbyang ba rnams phal cher rdor phreng ltar dang / mi bskyod pa la chu dbang mi sbyor bar rnam snang la chu dbang sbyor
bar mdzad/ don yod grub pa dril bu'i dbang gi rjes la/ mig thur sher phyin ma dang / me long rdo rje sems dpar bskyed cing mchod bstod/ de zhu ba las byung ba'i mig thur
dang me long gi dbang byed/ mi bskyod pa'i dbang dang 'brel bar lung bstan sngon la byas nas/ mchog tu gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor 'dir/ /zhes sogs kyi dbugs dbyung la/ oM badzra
sa twa satwaM sogs kyis dbang bskur bar mdzad do/ gzhan yang phyag mtshan gyi sngon du maNDal dang / slob dpon

gyi dbang gi gsol btab sbyar nas 'khor lo la sogs pa phyag mtshan bzhi'i dbang bskur/ de nas slob ma dbang stegs kyi steng du 'khod la nang dbang bskur/ slar phyir 'thon pa
la ye shes pa bcug gnas gsum byin gyis brlabs la dam tshig gsum byin pa rnams mdzad cing / lugs snga mar de dag mi mdzad la/ yang dbang bka' rnying ma'i lugs la slob dpon
gyi dbang dang / slob ma'i rig pa'i dbang rnams la nang dbang ma bshad gsar mar de kun la nang dbang bshad la/ gzhan yang snga mar dbang de rnams so sor lus dkyil 'god
par ma bshad cing / phyi mar nang dbang bskur ba'i rjes la slob ma dbang stegs kyi steng du 'khod nas rten dang brten pa'i lus dkyil la bkod/ ye shes pa bcug gnas gsum byin
gyis brlabs nas dbang bskur bar mdzad pa yin la/ dbang gong ma gsum ni gsar mar zung 'jug gsal ba nas kha bskangs pa bzhin mdzad la/ de dang snga ma'i lugs kyi dbang gong
ma gsum bskur ba'i tshig rigs mi 'dra ba mang du yod la/ gzhan yang lugs snga mar bum dbang thob nas dben pa gsum kar bsgom pa dang / gsang dbang thob nas sgyu lus dang
/ sher dbang thob nas 'od gsal dang / dbang bzhi pa thob nas zung 'jug bsgom par rtogs bskyed la gsungs/ phyi mar dbang gi rtogs bskyed la bum dbang thob nas bskyed rim
yan lag dang bcas pa bsgom du rung / gsang dbang thob nas rdo rje'i bzlas pa dang sems dben bsgom pa la dbang / shes rab dbang thob nas bdag byin gyis

brlabs pa'i rims pa bsgom pa la dbang / dbang bzhi pa thob nas 'od gsal dang zung 'jug gi rim pa bsgom pa la dbang bar gsungs pas snga phyi gnyis phyag len dang tshig rigs
mi 'dra ba ni mdor bsdus na de dag yin no/ /lugs snga ma 'dis chog bsgrigs gsal bar ston pa la/ rong tshe dbang grags kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog dang rdog ArYa de bas mdzad
pa'i dkyil chog yod par bshad cing / phyi ma 'di lag tu blang ba'i cho ga ni bla ma 'phags pas mdzad pa'i dkyil chog dang / phyis su ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun
dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i dkyil chog ye shes rgya mtsho sogs dang / de nyid gzhir bzhag gi phyag len phra mo tshun kyang zhib tu bkod pa'i snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog gzhan phan rgyas byed sogs du ma yod do/ /yang rang lugs kyi zin bris 'ga' zhig las/
bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i dkyil chog kyang gsar ma'i lugs kho na yin par bshad kyang / bu ston gyi 'di ni lugs snga phyi bsres pa zhig yin dgos sam snyam ste/ bu ston
la 'phags 'od kyis 'gos lugs kyi dbang sogs dbang bka' bdun po gcig tu bsres pa'i dbang rgyas pa zhig gnang nas brgyud pa 'dren pa na lugs srol bdun ka'i brgyud pa 'dren
par mdzad nas dbang bdun kar bsres pas na/ dkyil chog kyang tshul de bzhin du rtsom par rigs pas so snyam mo/ /des na bu ston gyi dkyil chog 'di sa lugs gtsang ma yin
min brtag dgos so/ /de rnams kyis sa lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa'i sgo nas

lugs de ji ltar dar ba'i tshul bstan zin pa ste/ bod yul du 'dus pa 'phags skor ji ltar byung tshul legs par bshad zin pa yin la/ gnyis pa ye shes zhabs lugs sogs lugs gzhan
bstan pa la yang / ye shes zhabs lugs kyi brgyud rim smos te de nyid ji ltar dar ba'i tshul dang / jo bo'i lugs kyi brgyud rim smos te de nyid ji ltar dar ba'i tshul dang
gnyis las/ dang po ni/ bod 'dir thog mar lo chen rin chen bzang pos/ paNDi ta shaddha ka ra warma la zhus pa'i gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang sogs dang / de'i rjes su
gnyos lo tsA ba yon tan grags kyis paNDi ta ba liM ta A tsArYa la zhus pa'i gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i bshad srol bzang po byung ba de nyid dang / rwa lo tsA ba
rdo rje grags kyis ngo bo puNya shrI la zhus pa'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dbang dang / gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis bla ma paN dha pa la zhus pa'i dbang sogs
mang du byung ba yin yang / deng sang bka' ma nub cing dar rgyas yod pa ni gnyan lo nas brgyud pa 'di nyid de/ de yang gnyan lo chen po des 'phags yul du byon nas ri sul
gyi rnal 'byor ma dang / bla ma paN dha ba sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ mdo sngags kyi chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab zhig dang / khyad par gsang ba 'dus pa ye shes zhabs
lugs kyi dbang dang gdams pa mang po zhig dang / 'dus pa'i chos skyong gnyan mgon chen po zhal bzhi pa'i chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa ma tshang ba med par spyan drangs kha'u
